談言

抗日與抵貨 284

— 賡

國難至今日，實已瀕於生死線上！﹁積極的軍事抵抗﹂與﹁消極的經濟制裁﹂，莫不知其爲答覆日帝國主義之唯一手段，匪但知之，而且多方面的再三聲明，﹁誓﹂必爲之，例如在上者對抗日之﹁誓詞﹂﹁誓師﹂﹁誓死守土﹂﹁誓不生還﹂，在下者對仇貨之﹁誓不買﹂﹁誓不賣﹂﹁誓不用﹂等等，且也，﹁誓﹂之爲﹁誓﹂，其重大意義，不僅在於肝胆照人，天地共鑒，而還含着一種幽默的妙用，足以大大的嚇一嚇日本。好像每一次每一回的﹁誓﹂，都是在指天劃地地對準日本說：﹁東洋小子！我這裏已在賭着咒了，﹁賭咒﹂和你拚了，小子還不怕麽？哼！﹁你試試看！﹂

無奈東洋人眞頑皮，眞混蛋，好像他已打聽淸楚這些有音無形，有氣無力的﹁賭咒﹂聲，與老太婆的咒鷄咒狗并無二樣，所以他始終抱定一種態度，咒憑你咒，幹由我幹，幹了勝利、還要像﹁爬在外衣上的白虱﹂，﹁又吃人又羞人﹂地把事實宣布出來，眞不怕氣煞賭咒之人也！

去年年底，各報曾有過這樣的記載：

﹁最近日幣價格低落，各地反日抵貨無形銷沉，日商爭相輸入各貨，冀得　　一攫萬金，總計一月來，本埠日貨輸入達萬噸左右，

又據最近日本大藏省，發表本年二月份對華貿易，日本之輸出（即我之輸入）計爲三千二百二十六萬三千元日金，三月份者雖尚未發表，但由此巨數類推，以及各商店生意興隆，全國太平景象證之，還是請日本大藏省大發慈悲，勿要發表的好，以免嚇壞了一般﹁愛國之心，未敢後人﹂的愛國分子！

在此抵貨的緊張月份，仇貨反輸入了這麽多，這一定是東洋科學新發明，把日貨暗中生了兩翼或四足，自動的會﹁飛﹂﹁跑﹂到我﹁不買﹂﹁不賣﹂仇貨的商店裏去，然後又分頭﹁飛﹂﹁跑﹂到我﹁不買﹂﹁不用﹂仇貨的好人家來了！所以以後抵制日貨之巨責，只好和某外交家所主張一般的，希望印度人去肩承着罷了！

至於﹁什麽誓，什麽誓﹂的抗日戰爭，又怎麽樣呢？那只消以遼吉黑熱四省的顯明事實爲﹁被加數﹂，再以近日各報所常見之有字的﹁闢謠﹂和無字的﹁黑方框﹂弦外之音爲﹁加數﹂，很簡單的一盤﹁加法﹂，便求得我們所欲求之眞正﹁答數﹂了！

兩化元之又一捷法 285

— 蔚

讀四月六日本刊見有歐陽君之﹁兩化元之七一五捷法﹂一文，算法精巧，至堪欽佩！惟拙意此種類似珠算飛歸之口訣，非熟讀殊難記憶，且計算時，因所牽涉之位數過多，不易應用，猶覺美中不足耳。兹得另一捷法，略述如左，以供讀者之研究。

緣吾人日常由銀兩折算銀元時，須以洋釐除銀兩數，因須應用除法，計算手續，較爲麻煩。依算理以甲數除乙數，與以甲數之倒數乘乙數，兩法所得結果完全相等（因Ａ－Ｂ＝Ｂ×Ｉ－Ａ），故欲由銀兩數折算銀元數，可以洋釐之倒數乘銀兩數，以免除除法手續之繁瑣。例如欲以規銀三百六十七兩，依法定洋釐七一五，折算銀元則用除法其式如下：銀兩數３６７

丨丨丨丨丨＝５１３２９元如用乘法其式如洋釐０·７１５

ＩＩ

下：銀兩數×丨丨＝３６７丨丨＝３６５×１·３洋釐０·７１５

９８６＝５１３·２９元蓋依法定洋釐七一五，則規銀一兩應合銀元一·三九八六元，故由銀兩折合銀元時，應以一·三九八六乘銀兩數，其理至明今洋釐旣係法定，必無變動，故此一·三九八六之數，亦固定不變。爲求計算手續簡捷起見，可將此數簡作一·四。按此簡數與原有之實數相差僅○·○○一四元，即在用一·四乘銀兩以求銀元數時，每銀一兩計多算銀元一厘四毫，百兩多算銀元一角四分，千兩多算銀元一元四角，於換算時可加改正。試仍以前題爲例，用捷法計算如下：３６７×１·４＝５１３·８０元５１３·８０丨（３·６７×·１４）＝５１３·８０丨·５１＝５１３·２９元前式中３·６７×·１４係由銀兩折合銀元用一·四乘銀兩時·多算銀元之數，故須減除之。此减除之數，其數字與前式上半式中之乘積相同，故無須計算，止須將小數移上三位，蓋所欲折成銀元之銀兩數，旣爲百位，則减除之數當爲角數也。

病中 286

— 萍

（一）死

生病不是我專利的事，每個病人的經騐中，無論僅僅是發寒熱之類，他們的意識中很容易浮起恐怕的﹁死﹂字。我的爸爸生病死了，我的表姊生病死了，我的朋友生病死了，我的生病豈能例外，許多可怕的影像，都聚集在帳門的四圍，我好像一會便能死去的一般，但是終於爬起床來了。一切可怕的死的影像，重驅出我記憶之外，被麵包代替了　的位置。除了自殺，死也並不怎樣容易吧？

（二）春

春飄到了人間，感傷的詩人唱出美麗詩句，綠柳碧桃更是歌頌的文字，我似乎記起應該掃墓的時候了。飄泊在海上將近五年，故鄉遠在數千里之外，爸爸墓上的靑草，是否還像我離别時的葱鬱，老母頭上恐怕將堆上如霜的白髮？每個春帶給我的是什麽？在年齡上增加記號，就是死亡的路程；春，你再能給我一個最後的希望嗎？汽車的聲音從窗外送來，告訴我這是到龍華掃墓去的。我倚在窗檻上，遙望西南，春，你再給我一個最後的希望吧！

1933.04.10

Enemy Retreats from Shimen Village Towards Shahe Village 1

Our Troops Cross Luozhuang in Pursuit

It Is Said That Shimen Village Remains Surrounded on All Sides by Our Troops

Our Main Force Is Deployed Along the Liujiang Railway and Anmin Village Line

Loud Cannon Fire Heard from Yuguan, Qinbu Refugees Return, Order Gradually Restored

(Beiping) According to transportation circles, the enemy at Shimen Village was repelled by our troops at 9:00 PM last night and retreated towards Shahe Village. Fierce fighting occurred along the way. Currently, our troops have crossed Shimen Village, advancing about seven or eight *li* to Luozhuang, and are pursuing the enemy, aiming to take advantage of the momentum to attack the Shahe Village line and drive the enemy back beyond Jiukou. He Zhuguo returned to Haiyang Town from Tanghe on horseback yesterday morning and then went to Beidaihe, taking a special train back to Luan County. Our vanguard, about 3,000 strong, is advancing from Shimen Village towards Shahe Village. The main force is deployed along the Liujiang Railway line and Anmin Village line. A certain artillery unit and a certain regiment of our army have been fully deployed to a certain location. The defenses of Haiyang Town and Qindao are extremely solid. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) Luanzhou telegram reports that there was no major fighting yesterday morning. The enemy reorganized its forces in the Dasha River area. At 3:00 PM, enemy reinforcements arrived and, in conjunction with the Iwata unit, launched a counterattack from Shimen Village towards Heishanwa, Qiuziyu, and Danjiagou. Our troops held firm at [missing characters] Village, engaging the enemy in fierce fighting. Our [missing characters] regiment successfully maneuvered around Liangjiashan and crossed the Yang[missing character] Shimen Village line, occupying Dingjiayu Mountain, cutting off the communication line between Shahe Village and Shimen Village. Our troops have pressed the attack to the vicinity of Shimen Village. The remaining enemy troops, unable to withstand the pressure, retreated from Liangjiashan and Shimen Village while fighting. Shimen Village has been surrounded on all sides by our troops and can be completely resolved. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) A visitor from Qindao reports that the Kailuan Mining Bureau and the Customs at Qindao have both received news of our troops' recapture of Shimen Village. Cannon fire is no longer frequently heard in Qinbu. Loud cannon fire is heard from Yuguan, as the battle line is far from Haiyang and Qindao. The villages along the Tanghe River and near Haiyang, such as Zhangzhuang, Miaozhuang, Cuizhuang, Zhao Zhuang, Qian Yuezhuang, and Hou Yuezhuang, were all destroyed by Japanese artillery fire, turning into scorched earth, a terrible sight. Refugees from various villages have taken refuge in the Shazishan area of Qindao. Yesterday, they began to return to their villages. Qinbu has gradually returned to its original state. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) Last night, our troops made contact with the enemy in the Xujiagou area. Most of our troops are intercepting the enemy at Shimen Village, Shahe Village, and Jiukou. Our troops have the upper hand, and the Japanese rebel army is retreating towards Jiukou. Japanese troops are responsible for the defense of the Shimen Village front. This morning, a large number of Japanese aircraft heavily bombed our advancing infantry. This afternoon, our troops clashed with the enemy in the Heishanyao area. He Zhuguo went to a certain location from Luanzhou this morning to direct the operations. A Japanese aircraft carrier is stationed eight *li* from Qindao, and the aircraft are responsible for reconnaissance and bombing along the Beining line. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) Qindao Customs reports that [missing characters] artillery units with more than two hundred pieces, [missing characters] four battalions of infantry, and [missing characters] two battalions of infantry launched a victorious counterattack at 5:00 AM yesterday, fighting fiercely all day. By 8:00 PM, they had recaptured Shimen Village. By midnight, they had advanced another seven or eight *li*. The Yuguan Customs heard loud cannon fire. (9th dispatch)

(Luanzhou) From the night of the 8th to noon on the 9th, there was contact between frontline sentries, but no major battle. The main force of the enemy at Shimen Village numbered over four thousand, constructing fortifications and setting up an airfield. One enemy troop train arrived early this morning, and the troops were deployed to Jiukou. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) Luan County telegram reports that more than one thousand Japanese troops are gathered in the Shimen Village area. The rebel troops of Li Jichun, Zheng Yanhou, and Zhao Lei, numbering more than two thousand, are extremely demoralized and show no sign of a counterattack. About five thousand Japanese, rebel, and Korean troops are gathered in the Heishanyao and Liujiahe area, constructing defenses in the area. The unit is designated as the Jing'an Guerrilla Force, organized with five men per squad, one Korean and four rebels, with the squad leader being Japanese. (9th dispatch)

(Luanzhou) From the night of the 8th to the night of the 9th, there was no major battle. There was occasional contact with scouts, but they were all repelled. About three thousand mixed Japanese and puppet troops are gathered at Shimen Village, with part of them near Oujiang, confronting our troops at Shangpingshan, Xiapinghshan, and Xiayu. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) The situation in the Qindao area has returned to what it was ten days ago. Enemy and our troops are in a stalemate between Shimen Village and Liujiang, and there is no fighting. The enemy is currently transferring reinforcements from the puppet Fengshan line to increase forces at Shimen Village. Our left-wing division has established contact with the Liujiang troops, and the front line is extremely solid. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) According to news from the Luan River, the vanguard of the Chinese army has reached a point three *li* from Shimen Village. Currently, the main force of the Chinese army is south of Liujiang, busily engaged in constructing defensive works to prevent a Japanese counterattack. The Japanese army is currently concentrating at Shimen Village, awaiting reinforcements from outside the pass. Yesterday, Japanese aircraft bombed the Chinese army positions in Haiyang Town and reconnoitered the area along the Luanzhou, Fengning, and Beining roads. Qinhuangdao is now calm, and the sound of cannon fire is no longer heard. (9th Reuters dispatch)

The Recapture of Anmin Village 2

(Beiping) The first line of enemy rebel troops attacking eastern Luanzhou consisted of the puppet Anti-Japanese National Salvation Army's First Army, led by Li Jichun, under which was the First Route Commander Yu Mingde, the Second Route Commander Zhang Jiao, the Third Route Commander Zhao Dazhong, the Fourth Route Commander Qian Baochang, and the Fifth Route Commander Zhao[missing character]. The second line consisted of Japanese veterans, and the third line consisted of two thousand puppet Rehe defense troops and more than seven hundred Japanese troops. Our army previously retreated to the Wangjialing and Wujiazhuang area for strategic reasons. On the night of the 6th, He Zhuguo arrived at a certain location in front to command the counterattack, ordering Liu's battalion to defend Qindao to the death, forbidding any to return alive. At dawn on the 7th, a part of our cavalry maneuvered to Anmin and Qinshan [missing character], encountering the [missing character] Maichang rebel troops passing through the area on horseback with three squads of soldiers. Our sentry immediately opened fire, killing [missing character] rebels and capturing the soldiers alive. The Qian rebel troops in Anmin Village panicked, and at the same time, our troops advanced on the left and right wings, occupying Anmin Village. On the night of the 8th, they successively recovered positions at Haiyang Town, Shimen Village, Anmin Village, and Ping'an Ying. The enemy was in a state of utter chaos, retreating towards the Shi River. Our troops are advancing to search for the enemy's remnants. The vanguard recovered the Tanghe position yesterday morning. There has been no contact today. (9th dispatch)

Japanese Atrocities in Rehe Territory 3

(Beiping) Military news reports that Japanese troops in Rehe territory and in the villages within Hebei Province outside the Great Wall are using the pretext of searching for righteous armies to forcibly seize livestock from the people's homes. The people there are living in misery and despair. Many men have taken refuge in the mountains, ambushing and killing Japanese troops. Many women have committed suicide due to being raped by Japanese troops. What is particularly tragic is that when Chinese women refused to hand over their cattle and sheep, arguing with the Japanese soldiers, the Japanese soldiers used their bayonets to stab several pregnant women to death, piercing their abdomens. Sergeant Hou of a certain regiment took the opportunity to escape when the Japanese troops retreated. He said that the Japanese troops did not treat our people as human beings. They were not given enough to eat every day and were locked in a room during rest periods. If they were slightly disobedient, they would be beaten with fists and kicked with rifle butts, and some were even shot to death. (9th dispatch)

Skirmish at Dalingkou 4

(Beiping) The [missing character] platoon of Zhu Jiqing's troops stationed at Dalingkou, while on sentry duty at 1:00 AM on the 5th, was suddenly attacked by dozens of enemy plainclothes troops. A fierce battle ensued with our sentries. Subsequently, our soldiers launched a head-on attack, repelling the enemy. The [missing character] platoon leader was seriously wounded in his left hand, and one soldier was wounded. Several hundred enemies are stationed at Cuijiabaozi, ten *li* from Dalingkou, constantly harassing the Daling Sekou area. (9th dispatch)

Two Trains of Enemy Wounded Arrive in Jinzhou 5

Linyu: According to intelligence reports, two trains of enemy wounded, carrying approximately four to five hundred wounded soldiers, arrived at Jin County from Wanjiatun Station on the 2nd. On the 8th, a troop train arrived at Qiansuo from the east, the number of soldiers unknown. After disembarking, they went to the Jiukou area. Also, the chief commander of the rebel army's vanguard is Zheng Yanhou, the deputy commander is Zhang Yaoting, the commander of the Second Army is Zhang Fenglin, and the commander of the First Cavalry Division is Han Xiaochen. (9th dispatch)

Enemy Attempted to Advance at Xifengkou but Failed 6

(Beiping) Xifengkou battle news: Starting at 7:00 AM on the 8th, the enemy used more than ten cannons to bombard the positions of our Li Regiment fiercely until 4:00 PM. At noon, the enemy used six or seven armored vehicles and more than a thousand infantrymen, relying on their artillery fire, to charge our positions. Our frontline officers and soldiers fought bravely, inflicting heavy casualties on the enemy, who then retreated. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) Someone from the front line reports that in the Lengkou battle, a certain soldier of Huang Regiment killed eighteen enemies with a single knife. However, wounded soldiers at the front have not received rice or wheat for three days, which is extremely tragic. (9th dispatch)

Enemy Aircraft Bomb Everywhere 7

(Beiping) Miyun telegram reports that at 10:00 AM this morning, one enemy aircraft flew to Miyun County to reconnoiter, dropping one bomb, but no one was injured. (9th dispatch)

(Luanzhou) This morning, enemy aircraft dropped bombs on Tanghe, Haiyang, and Shenhe. At noon, one aircraft flew to Luanzhou to reconnoiter. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) At 10:00 AM this morning, three Japanese aircraft dropped more than ten bombs on the Dashenhe and Xiaoshenhe area, causing unknown damage. (9th dispatch)

(Luanzhou) At noon on the 9th, three enemy aircraft dropped more than ten incendiary bombs on the north gate of Qian'an County, setting fire to civilian houses. The flames soared into the sky and had not been extinguished by Shenshi [3-5PM]. At noon, one enemy aircraft came to Luan County to reconnoiter for a long time. (9th dispatch)

(Luanzhou) This morning, three enemy aircraft reconnoitered both sides of the Tanghe River for more than an hour, dropping several bombs that missed their targets. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) Eleven enemy aircraft bombed Sahhe Bridge, and two bombed Santunying. A total of more than one hundred bombs were dropped at Sahhe Bridge, injuring forty-three soldiers and civilians and destroying more than one hundred and thirty civilian houses. Fifty-four bombs were dropped at Santunying, killing eighteen civilians and injuring more than thirty. No soldiers were injured. More than ninety civilian houses were destroyed. Half of the bombs dropped this time were particularly heavy, with craters about three meters deep and a radius of about three meters. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) Kailu telegram reports that this afternoon, one enemy aircraft flew to Chazitou Station, thirty *li* west of Luan County, to reconnoiter. One Japanese aircraft also arrived in Luan County. (9th dispatch)

(Beiping) Yesterday afternoon, one enemy aircraft circled over the Lulong and Liyi area and then left. (9th dispatch)

Linyu: In the past two days, enemy aircraft have come in formations of three to five to bomb our positions and to reconnoiter the rear. (9th dispatch)

Multiple Japanese Warships Spotted off Beidaihe 8

(Beiping) One Japanese aircraft carrier, three battleships, and a total of twenty destroyers and torpedo boats are currently present in the waters off Qindao and Beidaihe. (9th dispatch)

Japanese Side Induces and Deceives Mongolians, Central Government Actively Planning Response 15

(Nanjing) The Japanese side convened a meeting of Mongolian princes in Rehe, intending to deceive the Mongolian people through political means and achieve their ambition to seize Inner Mongolia. The central government should have a response to this. The Mongolian nationality has strong tenacity, and once their will is set, it is not easy to change. In this respect, there is no problem with the combination of Mongolians and Han Mongolians. Mongolians have been inclined toward the central government for more than a day, and in recent years, the central government has been more attentive to the protection of Mongolians than before. The Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission has sent Chun De to reside in the Chahar, Suiyuan, and Rehe area to contact the Mongolians and investigate their living conditions at any time, hoping that the central government and the Mongolians can communicate in a timely manner. No Mongolian princes should attend the Japanese meeting. Even if there are any, they will have to participate due to environmental pressure and will definitely not want to abandon the Mongolian-Han combination and be used by the Japanese. After receiving this information, the central government, in addition to telegraphically instructing the relevant parties to continue reconnaissance and report at any time, is now studying effective methods to stop it and will send appropriate personnel to Chahar, Suiyuan, and other places to have practical contact with Mongolian princes and Mongolians so that they can unite to prevent the Japanese army from invading. (9th dispatch)

(Nanjing) Bai Yanfeng, the representative of the Zuo League, went to Beiping on the 9th to report to the Mongolian princes and Zhuo Wang, De Wang, etc., staying in Ping, about the process of contact in Beijing, and to discuss and telegram the government to quickly decide on measures to deal with Mongolian affairs in order to prevent the violent Japanese from taking advantage of the situation. (9th dispatch)

As Soon as Other Generals Arrive

Chiang summoned senior generals from various provinces to Jiangxi to discuss bandit suppression and security in various provinces. The conference date will be determined after all the generals arrive. Chiang has meticulous plans and absolute certainty for suppressing bandits in Jiangxi. He hopes that Chiang can reside in Jiangxi for a long time to complete the task of suppressing bandits as soon as possible. Henan is calm, the roads are clear, and ninety counties have telephones. With convenient transportation, bandit suppression will naturally be smooth. (9th dispatch)

Current Affairs Commentary

British Prime Minister Visits America (Part 1) Letter 19

(1) The Sharpening of Conflicts Among European Countries

British Prime Minister MacDonald has accepted the invitation from the US President. He is scheduled to visit the United States to discuss future world economic problems and their solutions. The US State Department announced on April 7 that it would invite Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, French Premier Daladier, and German Chancellor Hitler to personally attend the World Economic Preparation Conference invited by Washington. The content of the meeting is not officially announced, but according to general observations and statements from officials, it will cover the following three main points. First, how to recover from the global economic panic, market contraction, and overproduction. Second, the arms race is an open secret. The expansion of air forces and the strengthening of land forces are being actively prepared from Western Europe to North America and East to the Pacific Ocean. Efforts should be made to resolve the issue or at least temporarily alleviate it. Third, war debts are a huge cancer between Europe and the United States. How should they be treated in order to be saved? The above three are the major topics to be discussed between the British Prime Minister and the US President. What is the current situation? What will be the future trends? All of them will have direct and indirect impacts on our country. I will briefly discuss them now.

Today's international political situation stands at a crossroads. Where to go and what to do? Political authorities in various countries are struggling to find a definite and appropriate decision. Even experts have diverse opinions, each asserting their own views. In the international arena, there are two major oppositions: capitalism and socialism, which are incompatible with each other. In Europe alone, Germany and Italy are making every effort to develop their unique nationalism, eager to break free from their current difficulties. Germany is eager to break the shackles of the Treaty of Versailles and open up new avenues for the German people. Italy is a poor country with scarce land, but it wants to divide Central European hegemony and gain a leading position on the Mediterranean coast. Therefore, Germany and Italy are allied to threaten France. The British Empire, which is close to but not connected to the European continent, was the world's leading hegemon for fifteen years. However, after the European War, Germany suffered a major setback, and France became the dominant force, threatening to subdue the whole of Europe. The United Kingdom, adhering to its traditional teachings, never wants a single strong country in Europe. Therefore, when Germany was at its peak, having a force confronting Britain in Africa and East Asia, Britain allied with France to contain it. Now, France can politically lead Europe and, economically, even outstrips Britain in terms of gold reserves. At this time, for the sake of its own future, the United Kingdom cannot but be friendly to Germany and Italy and alienate its former ally, France. Therefore, MacDonald flew across the English Channel to discuss arms reduction with the Black Shirt Prime Minister and proposed the Four-Power Pact. France, facing these three-pronged threats, can only protect its security and expand its national strength by linking with the Little Entente to jointly contain Germany and Italy. On the other hand, it shows goodwill to the Soviet Union to contain Britain. Thus, the intricate situation becomes more complex, and the world situation becomes even more gloomy.

(2) The Future of the World Economy

Since the rise and growth of capitalism, economic panic has been a cyclical recurrence. However, the duration of the panic has never been so long as this time, and the damage has never been so severe. Moreover, the economic panic is still in the process of development. In economically developed countries such as the United States and Germany, production restrictions have reached 70% to 80%, and price drops have reached one-third to one-quarter. How can the suffering masses endure such a sight? Even the wealthy (regardless of any country) have huge amounts of monetary capital idling without interest. Only speculation is still active, while real investment is completely frozen. Here are some production figures and prices at the end of 1929 and 1932 as examples.

Production Quantity　　　　　　　　　　　　　　　Price

United States　　(1) 47%　　　(1) 47%

United States　　(1) 16%　　　　(1) 37%

France　　(1) 32%　　　(1) 36%

Germany　　(1) 44%　　　(1) 31%

Italy　(1) 30%　　　　(1) 35%

In the early spring of this year, coupled with the financial panic in the United States, capitalist countries are really caught in an endless tragedy. As for the ways to rescue, the conclusion from comprehensive research in various aspects is only two ways. One is to open up the current protectionist tariff barriers of various countries. The other is to stabilize the standard system, so that money can be used for circulation and there is no stagnation.

In fact, the current countries, from political authorities to industrialists in the opposition, have undergone considerable training and have a considerable understanding and recognition of the current crisis. How can they not know that the source of the economic panic is definitely not so simple, and the planning to rescue the panic is not necessarily so easy. The opposite reason for the increase in tariffs in various countries is self-sufficiency within the country, while the development of overseas markets has not been relaxed in half a step. The reason why it does not help to overproduce but leads to a shrinking market is that the general purchasing power within the country has declined abnormally due to extreme exploitation. The rise of rational management has led to chronic unemployment that cannot be saved (the expansion of mechanical power has reduced manpower, and the number of unemployed has increased). The rise of colonial capital has narrowed the overseas consumer market. The more overseas investment, the more the domestic industry will be depressed. In addition, the strong revelation of the Soviet Union's planned economy has made the societies of various countries feel more uneasy. The economic foundation is becoming more unstable due to the low level of consumption. As for the stability of the monetary system, it only has some impact on circulation, but it does not help much to the entire economic panic.

American International Peace Organization's Annual Report Deeply Criticizes Japan's Actions 20

Japanese Military Clique Controls Government and People

Using the Mask of Self-Defense to Carry Out Aggression

(Washington) Dr. Butler, Director of the Carnegie Endowment for International Peace, in his annual report, expressed deep anxiety about the situation in the Far East, saying that the situation there is in extreme turmoil and decline. He also said that it is now increasingly clear that Japan is now completely under the control of the military, causing its government and people to be led into war under the mask of self-defense. Such actions are enough to make Japan lose the sympathy and trust of the world. (8th National News Agency)

Japan-Netherlands Arbitration Treaty 21

(Nanjing) Japan's new diplomatic policy after withdrawing from the League of Nations is to establish friendly relations with various countries individually. The first step is for Saito Hiroshi, the Japanese ambassador to the Netherlands, to conclude a Japan-Netherlands arbitration treaty with the Netherlands. According to a report received by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs on the 8th, the draft of the treaty has been prepared and will soon be signed. The main points of the draft treaty are as follows: (1) Regarding the Japan-Netherlands Navigation Treaty, and the statement supplementing the special rights of the Netherlands in the Pacific region in 1921, it is agreed that the fundamental policy for resolving disputes between Japan and the Netherlands; (2) In case of disputes over legal issues and the interpretation of existing treaties, they shall be submitted to arbitration in The Hague; (3) If the dispute concerns the independent interests or reputation of the two contracting countries, and also concerns the interests of a third country, it shall be resolved in accordance with specific regulations. (9th Domei News Agency)

Tensions Suddenly Rise Over the Chinese Eastern Railway Issue 22

(Changchun) The dispute over the Chinese Eastern Railway is intensifying. "Manchukuo" has used force to prevent the direct connection of freight trains passing through the Russian border areas of eastern and western Manchuria. In fact, the connection of goods passing through Siberia and the Chinese Eastern Railway has been severed. If the Soviet Union orders the Red Russian workers of the Chinese Eastern Railway to strike as a retaliatory measure, "Manchukuo" will accuse it of interrupting international routes and take other measures to counter it, so the issue has suddenly become tense. (9th Domei News Agency)

After the Ministry discovered this, it sent several telegrams to Zhang to stop him, but received no reply. In addition to separately submitting petitions to the Supreme Military Authority and the Executive Yuan, to file a negotiation with the French side, it is imperative to cancel this illegal contract that confuses the jurisdiction system and sells it beyond authority, and return the original property to the Navy before it is over. Our Country Adopts Both Conscription and Militia Systems 27

Zhou Yawei Discusses the Key Points of the Military Service Law

(Nanjing) Zhou Yawei, Deputy Director of the Training and Supervision Department, talked about the points to note when formulating the military service law in our country, saying that since the National Army Reorganization Conference in the 16th year of the Republic of China stipulated that the national standing army should be 800,000, if this number is taken as the standard, then calculating our country's 400 million population, it is two per thousand. For example, if a village has 1,000 households, only two people need to serve, which is of course difficult. As for the system to be adopted, which one is suitable and which kind of deployment is easy to implement, judging from our national conditions, it seems that the militia system is prone to abuses, because it is compulsory in nature, and it is difficult to guarantee that the people handling it will not use extortion and intimidation. Therefore, our country seems to be suitable to adopt both the conscription and militia systems. When the Central Political Council discussed the principles a few days ago, it has been decided that the standing army will be the conscription system, and the conscripted soldiers will be the militia system. Before implementation, the first step should be a general survey of the national population. Some say that our country's economy is difficult, and the conscription system requires huge expenses, which are difficult to bear. In fact, this is not the case. The so-called national economy should be calculated together with the national economy. If the conscription system is used, there will be military pay, and the national economy will be slightly richer. If the conscription system is used, it will easily affect the national economy. If the national economy is exhausted, the national economy will be difficult, which is a related relationship. Therefore, the conscription system will not affect the national finances. However, there is one important issue, that is, all the improvements of the army, such as treatment, diet, hygiene, etc., and the improvement of the army's reputation and status, in order to break the people's aversion to the army and make everyone happy to serve, then the implementation of the military service law will be very promising. (9th Special Dispatch)

The Legislative Yuan is Drafting a New Criminal Law 28

No Need to Set Up a Special Court for Corruption

(Nanjing) The Criminal Law Committee of the Legislative Yuan is proceeding with the drafting of a new criminal law and is scheduled to be completed by the end of June. The general provisions have been drafted, and the specific provisions are still under discussion. It is also planned to send several committee members to various places to investigate the situation of the courts and the people as the basis for drafting the specific provisions. As for punishing corruption, after discussion by the committee, it is believed that there should be provisions in the criminal law, and there is no need to set up a special court. For disciplinary aspects, the amount of fines should be determined according to the degree of corruption, and the most serious offenders may be sentenced to death, so that corrupt officials will have some caution. (9th Special Dispatch)

Washington Conference and World Economic Recovery

Key Points of Roosevelt's Plan 64

Reduce Tariffs, Stabilize Exchange Rates, Raise Prices

International Trade Could Increase by Three Hundred Billion Annually

MacDonald and Herriot to Sail Together to the U.S.

Washington, 8th (National Telegram) – (1) Substantially reducing tariffs to allow countries to sell surplus goods, (2) stabilizing international exchange rates, and (3) universally abandoning nationalistic economic policies will be the core of discussions between the U.S. and representatives from various countries. If these fundamental principles can be agreed upon, the U.S. government estimates that international trade could increase from the current 160 billion gold dollars to 500 billion gold dollars annually.

The State Department believes these negotiations can be concluded before the World Economic Conference convenes in London on June 15th. Secretary of State Hull stated today that it is time to end high tariffs, promote international trade, and lead the world out of the mire of economic nationalism. Since the European war, the entire world has been trapped in this mire, unable to extricate itself. He also said he believes President Roosevelt is prepared to propose proposals and concessions that all countries can agree to.

While the President's plan has not yet been released, reliable sources indicate it will likely include the following: (1) revising all tariffs, even eliminating some, to promote international trade; (2) stabilizing international exchange rates, preferably gradually moving towards a universal return to the gold standard; (3) raising prices. However, Secretary of State Hull and those close to the President have not indicated how this will be achieved. Recently, there have been many proposals to inflate the currency, but the Secretary of State and most cabinet members oppose this. The President has not yet expressed his position.

The State Department received a telegram today stating that British Prime Minister MacDonald and former French Premier Herriot may travel to the U.S. together on the Berengaria ship. Herriot has accepted his appointment as the leader of the special envoy to the U.S. and is expected to depart from Southampton on that ship.

Before MacDonald and others arrive in the U.S., the President will send a message to Congress requesting broad powers to negotiate tax agreements separately with each country. With this authority, the President can freely discuss and accept or reject proposals from various countries and propose reciprocal treaties.

It is reported that the U.S. government is directly inviting only Britain, Italy, Germany, China, Japan, and the major Latin American countries. For other countries, it is stated that the U.S. welcomes joint consultations through the usual diplomatic channels. It is expected that European representatives will first discuss with the President, as Roosevelt firmly believes that cooperation between Europe and the U.S. can lead the economic recovery of the world. Although the economic situation in Latin America will affect trade between both Europe and the U.S., it will primarily affect the U.S. Therefore, discussions with South American experts will take place after consultations with other countries are completed, focusing mainly on stabilizing exchange rates.

Washington, 8th (National Telegram) – A recent survey of members of both the House and Senate regarding attitudes towards currency inflation reveals that if the proponents of inflation can agree on a single plan and have the President champion it, it could pass by a majority. Otherwise, without presidential leadership, such a plan will at least be temporarily shelved. It is rumored that those close to the President now believe that a carefully considered and well-managed inflation plan may be feasible. Secretary of State Hull, Agriculture Secretary Wallace, and Labor Secretary Perkins are also reportedly leaning towards this view, while other cabinet members oppose currency inflation. The President and Treasury Secretary Woodin remain silent but are reportedly opposed to inflation at this time.

Herriot Represents France 65

Paris, 9th (Havas) – Former Premier Herriot has agreed to represent France in Washington to discuss world economic issues with President Roosevelt. President Roosevelt stated that he hoped that when MacDonald visits the U.S., France would also send a highly respected individual to Washington to exchange views. All economic and financial matters should be discussed to prepare for the World Economic Conference. Therefore, French Premier Daladier and Foreign Minister Paul-Boncour requested former Premier Herriot to undertake this important task. Herriot's cabinet was overthrown last December due to disagreements with Congress regarding the repayment of war debts to the U.S. His appointment to visit the U.S. is welcomed by Washington.

Paris, 9th (Havas) – Herriot is traveling to the U.S. in the capacity of a "free observer," and will therefore not make any promises. However, all important information will be reported to the French government so that the government can understand the truth and decide on measures regarding the issues discussed at the White House, especially the war debt issue.

Washington, 9th (Havas) – Washington is pleased with the news that Herriot will represent France in the U.S. President Roosevelt has not yet decided on the attitude France should take. Political circles hope France can soon repay the war debts that were due on December 15th of last year. It is generally believed that Congress will grant the President the power to handle war debts, especially the war debts due on June 15th of this year.

London, 8th (Reuters) – According to Berlin sources, German Ambassador to the U.S. Dr. Luther and another embassy official will represent Germany. Dr. Luther is well-versed in Germany's economic difficulties and world affairs, so the German cabinet selected him as their representative so that German Chancellor Hitler or Foreign Minister Neurath do not have to visit Washington D.C. in person. The Italian government has not yet made a decision regarding sending a representative to the U.S., but it is expected that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini, who has not left Italy since 1923, will likely not participate personally.

Tokyo, 9th (Den-tsu) – Regarding the upcoming preliminary meeting for the World Economic Conference, the U.S. Undersecretary of State verbally invited Japan to participate on the afternoon of the 7th through Ambassador Debuchi to the U.S. According to the telegram received by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, the invitation included the following: "The President intends to personally meet with representatives of major countries to discuss preparations for the World Economic Conference and has already issued invitations to various countries. This meeting will touch upon disarmament issues, and it is hoped that your government will also send an important official as a representative."

Animal Gender Can Be Predetermined 66

New Invention by Soviet Professor

(Reuters, 9th, Moscow) Professor Koltsov, Director of the Moscow Animal Breeding Institute, claims to have invented a new method by which the gender of animals can be predetermined. He has created an electrical procedure to separate male and female sperm. If one desires to produce a male offspring, the mother is injected with a liquid that isolates the female sperm. If one desires a female, the opposite is done. The results are as intended. He has tested this method on female rabbits three times and has been successful in each instance.

It has been decided to accept this offer and instructions will be sent to Ambassador Debuchi on the 10th, replying that Japan will participate in the discussions. The government's representatives should address the issues of war debts and disarmament. It is uncertain whether Prime Minister Saito or a member of the cabinet will represent Japan in the U.S. However, given the preliminary discussions will be held on the 22nd and 23rd, it will be impossible to arrive in time. Consequently, Ambassador Debuchi will be appointed, assisted by Finance Official Tsushima. However, as the U.S. President will meet with each country's representatives separately, arriving by the 22nd or 23rd is not required. It is also possible that another important official will be sent, and this is currently being considered. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has instructed Ambassador Debuchi to report in detail.

Tokyo, 9th (Den-tsu) – The International Economic Conference will be held before July 25th. Starting June 10th, preliminary discussions will be held in Washington by the major countries. The Japanese government, with the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and Ministry of Finance at its center, has established a committee to discuss countermeasures. The general policy adopted is as follows: (1) Although the issue of war debts is not directly related to Japan, Japan will fully assist the economic conference to help the world overcome the current economic downturn, in cooperation with various countries. However, regarding the issue of disarmament, Japan will adhere to its established policy, namely, upholding the contents of the Japanese proposal submitted to the Geneva General Disarmament Committee. (2) Regarding international economic policy, Japan will advocate the following points to achieve coordination: (A) Based on enabling a return to the gold standard, internationally adjust prices and economic problems. (B) Restore the price of silver. (C) In order to regulate the movement of capital, strive to ease exchange rate restrictions. (D) To ensure freedom of trade and thoroughly realize it, seek international coordination on tariff policies.

Hull's New Trade Policy 67

Washington, 9th (Havas) – Secretary of State Hull declared to the press that the commercial policies that the world has adhered to for more than a decade must be completely overturned today. Hull continued that the development of economic nationalism is partly the responsibility of the United States. The economic panic has prevented world commerce from proceeding, and the United States has been the first to be affected. Currently, the United States feels it is appropriate to adopt a more sound and constructive policy. The U.S. government has no bizarre ambitions. What it seeks is only to overcome the difficulties. Currently, there is only one way out: to abandon the policy of excessive protection of domestic goods and allow foreign goods to be sold within its borders, without exclusively expecting other countries to purchase domestic goods.

Washington, 8th (Reuters) – Secretary of State Hull told reporters today that the primary goal of the United States in future economic discussions is to lead the world out of the predicament of economic nationalism. In recent years, countries around the world have revised their tax laws and competed with each other, causing great harm. The United States is one of the creators of this situation and one of the most severely impacted. In the past few years, U.S. foreign trade has decreased by a significant amount of six hundred billion dollars. The goal of this conversation is to seek a general compromise on the principles of reducing tax rates and abolishing exchange rate restrictions. Due to time constraints, quantity-based tax rates will be left to each country to determine on its own. As for practical solutions and detailed methods, they will be discussed at the upcoming World Economic Conference. According to today's news, Canada and Mexico have been invited by the U.S. to send representatives to participate in the discussions.

Beer and America 69

Two Days of Sales Sufficient to Float a Battleship

Tens of Thousands of Unemployed People Find Work

New York, 9th (Reuters) – According to observers skilled in calculations, if domestic breweries can produce legal beer to meet the constant demand, the beer sold on Friday and Saturday would be sufficient to float two battleships. In any event, the beer sold in the first twenty-four hours after the end of Prohibition in the United States was sufficient to float one battleship. At least seventy million people in twenty-one states and the District of Columbia happily drank, consuming one million to one and a half million barrels of beer, and local and central governments each received several million dollars in taxes. Although factories produced a lot of beer, it was still not enough to meet demand. However, the police have not seen any incidents of public drunkenness. The brewing and sale of beer has enabled tens of thousands of unemployed people to find work, and there is a general feeling of optimism about the recovery of commerce everywhere. Railways transporting large quantities of beer have also indirectly benefited. It is expected that the opening of new breweries will absorb several hundred thousand unemployed workers. In New York alone, revenue from brewing and selling beer licenses has reached two hundred thousand dollars.

British and Australian Flight Record Competition 70

(Reuters, 9th, London) Twenty-three-year-old Miss Batten, following Italian Robiano, is now attempting to fly from England to Australia. This morning at 6:35, the lady flew to Paris alone in a Moth aircraft that previously belonged to the British Crown Prince. If this trip is successful, she will be the second woman to fly solo between England and Australia. The first woman was Mrs. Mollison, also known as Amy Johnson, who completed this journey in 1930.

(Reuters, 9th, Rome) Italian aviator Robiano departed from Lympne Airfield in England yesterday, hoping to break the flight record from England to Australia. He arrived in Bari, Italy, on the southeast coast, at 7:18 last night, as scheduled. At dawn today, he continued towards Aleppo Island in Arabia.

Saito and the Japanese Political Situation 71

Fascist Dictatorship and Parliamentary Politics

The Key Lies in Saito's Advance and Retreat

Tokyo, 9th (Japan Alliance) – Some in political circles observe that a political change will definitely occur when Finance Minister Takahashi resigns at the end of April or the beginning of May. However, the movement to implement measures to extend the Saito cabinet's life in various forms is now attracting considerable attention. That is, those around Prime Minister Saito and the heads of the Minseito party, bureaucratic factions, and members of the House of Peers are running around seeking to extend the life of the current cabinet. Furthermore, senior statesmen in the Imperial Court also hope that political changes will not occur. It is said that when Privy Council Chairman Kuratomi met with Prime Minister Saito, Kuratomi stated that he would overcome all difficulties and strive to remedy the current situation. Therefore, when Justice Minister Oyama submitted his resignation, Saito uniquely sought an Imperial Rescript, with the Prime Minister proceeding from such a reputation with a firm resolve. The reasons for wanting to extend the life of the current cabinet are roughly as follows: the Saito cabinet's mission is to remove the danger of Japanese politics falling into a fascist dictatorship after the May 15th Incident, that is, to respect parliamentary politics, to request both the Seiyukai and Minseito parties to join the cabinet, and to work to remove social unrest. They also opened two parliamentary sessions, dealt with rural issues, and also, by going through the parliament, had 230 million of the great budget pass, for protection of the "Manchukuo," and implemented the withdrawal from the League of Nations. However, international relations after withdrawing from the League of Nations are deemed very important, and the credibility of political parties has not yet been restored. If the Saito cabinet were to fall, it would be very difficult to return to constitutional normalcy. Therefore, it would be better to maintain the current state of the current cabinet, and at the same time strive to restore the credibility of the political parties, and only after gaining confidence in the return to constitutional normalcy can the current cabinet be dissolved. These reasons are now resonating with various parties in political circles, so the so-called life extension movement of the cabinet may hold hope.

Tokyo, 9th (China Alliance) – Army Minister Araki will visit Finance Minister Takahashi tomorrow to test Takahashi's attitude towards the future Japanese political situation and to specifically deliberate on the huge military expenditure budget passed by the 64th Diet session and the earnest consolidation of various pursuit budgets. Because the fate of the current cabinet is already pressing on the issue of Finance Minister Takahashi's departure, the meeting between the two ministers tomorrow is particularly noteworthy to the world.

Luan Dong Our Army's Defensive Lines Are Solidified 72

Fierce Battle at Haiyang Town for Three Days and Nights

Even More Intense Battles Expected

Special Dispatch from Beiping: The Japanese army has changed its strategy, invading Luan Dong and Rehe simultaneously, putting pressure on both the east and west lines. Our army's battle plans have also changed slightly in response. Here is a report on the situation in Luan Dong:

At the beginning of the tense Luan Dong battles, He Yingqin, chairman of the Beiping Military Affairs Commission, telegraphed important front-line generals to Beiping to discuss strategy. Song Zheyuan, Yu Xuezhong, Pang Bingxun, Gao Guizi, Wang Yizhe, and others responded and arrived in Beiping one after another. After discussions, everyone agreed that the Japanese army had changed its strategy, focusing on Luan Dong and Rehe, and our army's defenses had to be adjusted accordingly. It was decided to redeploy the Luan Dong troops, allocating a portion of the troops from the various passes of the Great Wall to reinforce Luan Dong. After the meeting, He immediately issued orders to mobilize the troops that day. The troops transferred consisted of approximately three units, focusing on the area north of the railway. After this reorganization, the defensive lines should be more solid.

The Japanese army's attempts to invade Luan Dong included, in addition to the 14th Division and the puppet army led by Li Jichun, the transfer of the Hattori and Suzuki brigades from the Xifengkou area. The pretext for their invasion was that over ten Japanese soldiers were killed by our garrison while scouting ahead at Shimen Village. In reality, the Japanese army deliberately provoked the incident to justify their invasion. Since the start of the fighting, the Japanese army first occupied Shimen, then split into two routes to invade westward, one crossing the Liujiang River to attack Haiyang Town, and the other attacking Tanghe Tiemazhuang from Shihe Hongwadian. Haiyang Town is an important town on the eastern front, and both sides attached great importance to it. At 9:00 a.m. on the 3rd, the Japanese army advanced along the Liujiang Railway towards Haiyang Town, and another unit attempted to approach Qidao from the southeast of Anminzhai. They were met with a head-on attack by our army, and a fierce battle ensued for a day and night, resulting in heavy casualties on both sides. On the 4th, enemy reinforcements arrived, and Haiyang Town was temporarily lost. However, our army counterattacked and immediately recaptured it. On the 5th, the Japanese army regrouped and, on one hand, sent over 5,000 troops to invade Haiyang again, and on the other hand, sent aircraft to bomb Qian'an, Lulong, and Luanzhou to threaten our rear. The fighting around Haiyang Town became even more intense. After two days and one night of bloody battle and over ten hand-to-hand combat encounters, our army eventually withdrew yesterday (the 6th) due to strategic considerations. This morning (the 7th), He Zhuguo personally went to the front line to supervise the battle and ordered reinforcements from the rear to launch a general counterattack along the entire front line. Fierce battles occurred around Lipanzhuang near Haiyang Town and Wangjialing on the Pingyu Avenue. From morning to noon, our army made significant progress, with the vanguard having crossed Dawangzhuang. On the Tanghe front, the important areas of Wujiazhuang were also recaptured. Furthermore, five Japanese aircraft bombed the area between Qinhuangdao and Haiyang Town this morning. Due to international relations, the Japanese marines did not dare to land on Qinhuangdao, which remained calm. However, the Japanese army's invasion of Luan Dong focused on the area north of the railway, and they claimed that they would not stop until they occupied Luan Dong. Our army is determined to resist the enemy and has deployed large reinforcements. Even more intense main force battles are expected to occur within days.

Reports from the front lines over the past few days included the following: (1) On the Haiyang front, the headquarters of a certain army sent a telegram to Beiping this morning (the 7th) reporting on the fierce battle in Haiyang Town. The telegram stated, "Over a thousand enemy troops fiercely attacked Haiyang Town at dawn. Our cavalry regiments led by Wang, Shi, Xu, Liu, and the Ba battalion of the Jin regiment fought bravely against the enemy. They have not rested since yesterday. The enemy has reinforced with over two thousand troops and over twenty artillery pieces along the Liujiang Road. Our army is still calmly responding, killing two to three hundred enemies. Haiyang has finally been recaptured by our army. The remaining enemy troops are actively resisting. In this battle, our army fought fiercely for two days and nights under enemy fire, repeatedly advancing and retreating. The blood stained Haiyang, and the white bones and corpses were extremely tragic. Our officers and soldiers suffered the loss of a cavalry major company commander, over ten platoon leaders, and over two hundred soldiers." The enemy fled north of Haiyang. (5) Our cavalry □ unit is currently attacking the enemy at Daxiaolizhuang." (3) On the Shimenzhai front, He Zhuguo telegraphed Beiping today, stating, "Since the morning of the 31st of last month, the Iwata detachment of the enemy at Jiunmenkou, in coordination with artillery, advanced on our Shahezhai positions and attacked fiercely several times, but were repelled by our garrison. Chiang Inspects Troops in Fuzhou 73

The Red Bandits on All Routes Have Been Repelled

Provincial Defenses are Consolidated and Rumors are Allayed

Nanchang Dispatch: Zhu and Mao recently gathered the forces of Luo Binghui of the pseudo-Western Fujian Military District, Fang Zhimin of the pseudo-Jiangxi-Zhejiang-Fujian Military District, Chen Yi of the pseudo-Southern Jiangxi (i.e., Central District) Military District, Li Tianzhu of the pseudo-Jiangxi-Hunan Military District, as well as pseudo-independent army divisions, guerrilla advancement teams, etc., in the central section of the Gan River and at the junction of eastern and southern Jiangxi. After several hours of bloody battle, the bandits were defeated and retreated to Jinxi. In Yihuang and Le'an, the national army's various columns still guarded their original defenses, and there were no major changes in the front line. In Yongfeng, from the 2nd to the 4th, more than ten thousand of the pseudo-1st Army Corps besieged the county town. Sun Lianzhong's division's brigade stubbornly defended the city. On the evening of the 4th, they launched a surprise attack out of the city, ambushing the bandits and repelling them. As for the bandits in the Xingan area, because the bandits in Fuzhou did not make any progress, they dared not penetrate further. More than ten thousand bandits were discovered yesterday in Qiqin, more than fifty li from Xingan. The national army has transferred capable troops to block them along the Gan River from [missing text]. The Zhangshu area is like an outer city wall of the provincial capital, and a certain unit is deployed there. At the same time, the [missing text] independent brigade has arrived in Nanchang, and the city defense works attached to the city are extremely solid. Since Chiang's arrival, rumors have been allayed. (April 9th)
