Sino-Portuguese Cup Football Match: China Achieves First Victory 197

Portugal Loses 7-2

Over Seven Thousand Spectators Enjoyed a Splendid Performance

Sun Jinshun and Li Yichen Excelled in Shooting

The Sino-Portuguese Cup football match, which has a long history, was revived this year. The first match took place yesterday at 3 PM at the Chinese Baseball Field. Despite the cloudy weather and continuous spring rain, the audience turnout was still very enthusiastic. Father Road was bustling, and cars jammed the streets. The stands around the field were filled, reaching over seven thousand spectators. Both teams were well-organized, and the performance was splendid. Cheers and shouts sounded like ten thousand horses galloping and mountains collapsing. In the end, China defeated Portugal by a large margin of 7-2. The performances of both sides were extremely exciting, but due to the heavy rain, the field was waterlogged and slippery, hindering running. The ball, soaked in mud and water, was excessively heavy, making it difficult to run fast or kick far, which was a slight imperfection. The details of the match are recorded as follows:

Strength of Both Teams: Portugal has a well-established reputation and is indeed extraordinary. Although they lost, their performance was still commendable. Gu Shitan, Remy Di, and Kola Sa, among others, were exceptionally brave. For the Chinese team, Chen Zhenhe did not play, and Wan Xianghua took the left wing. The forwards worked diligently like a machine, and the defense was tight and impeccable. The goal-scoring skills of Sun Jinshun and Li Yichen were particularly praiseworthy. The lineups of both sides are as follows:

Chinese Team:

Zhou Xianyan, Li Ning, Wang Shusen, Shang Guanxun, Liang Shutang, Feng Yunyou, Tu Kaiyuan, Wan Xianghua, Sun Jinshun, Li Yichen, Chen Jiaqiu, Chen Yutian

Portuguese Team:

Marcel P, Gu Shitan (replaced by Ge Tielie), A Remy Di (replaced by Gu Shitan), A Kola Sa, Remy Di (replaced by A Gu Shitan), Hukui Na (replaced by Gao Shannu), Na Te, Ti Na, H Kola Sa, Lang Ge'er, Luolai

China Suffers Initial Setback: China kicked off first, attacking aggressively. Portugal pressed aggressively, displaying extraordinary bravery. China defended effectively, remaining unshaken. Li Huochen and Sun Zhushun led counterattacks but returned without success. Portugal encroached from the flank, and Luolai passed the ball from the baseline in front of the goal. Kola Sa, about seven or eight away from the goal, received the ball and shot, expecting to score, but it was blocked by Zhou Xianyan, a close call indeed. China thought they could rest easy, but one wave followed another. The Portuguese army attacked through the middle, passing the ball several times before Kola unleashed a powerful shot. The ball grazed the goalpost and entered the net. Zhou Xianyan fell to the ground but failed to save it, resulting in a loss of one goal. The audience was stunned.

Equalizing with Two Goals: After China conceded a goal, they kicked off from the center, attacking directly into the Portuguese territory. The front line was coordinated and responsive. However, due to the slippery ground, they struggled to maintain control. Feng Yunyou advanced backward, and amidst the chaotic scrum, Lao Feng executed a surprise attack, scoring a goal in return. From then on, China's momentum grew stronger. Wan Xianghua charged along the flank but was blocked by the enemy. He immediately lobbed the ball to Sun Jinshun, who sprinted forward, dribbling the ball towards the goal. However, he was again blocked by Gu Shitan, who then passed the ball to Li Yichen. Li succeeded in one go, scoring another goal, making it 2-1.

Another Goal: After that, Wan Xianghua once made a solo incursion, attacking the goal without success. If he had passed the ball to Li Yichen, who was waiting in front of the goal, a goal would have been certain. After a long scrum, Chen Yutian launched an attack from the flank, lobbing the ball towards the center. Yichen got the ball but lost it due to the slippery ground. Sun Jinshun charged forward and scored. Yichen was already offside, but the referee, being far behind, failed to observe closely. China thus gained an advantage with a score of 3-1. The Portuguese army repeatedly attempted to score, shooting many times, but fortunately, Zhou Xianyan's saves were effective, and the interception of the Li and Wang generals were thorough, leaving no room for error, so the Portuguese army could do nothing.

Each Scores Once: After the break, for the first ten minutes, neither side could find an opportunity to score, and there were few close calls. However, the momentum was still strong, and the spirit was consistent, so the interest did not diminish. Then, Li Yichen penetrated deep into the side of the goal and returned the ball in front of the goal. Sun Jinshun swept forward but missed. Soon after, Sun Jinshun had another opportunity and finally scored. The ball flew into the corner of the goal in an arc, which was very beautiful. Both sides fought with more and more spirit, and the delicate voices of the audience never stopped. The noble female guests in the one-yuan seats were ecstatic and watched with great interest, and their delicate voices and shouts added a lot of color to the stadium. Suddenly, the entire Portuguese team invaded the Chinese territory. The Chinese defense worked hard to resist, twisting into a ball, and Zhou Xianyan finally broke free and threw the ball out, turning danger into safety. But Kola Sa made a comeback and shot a quick goal, hitting the target, making it 4-2.

Three Consecutive Goals: Afterwards, the Portuguese army's arrogance slightly weakened. Although everyone was still working hard and competing, the front line showed signs of chaos, indicating they were unable to hold on. Li Yichen and Sun Jinshun of China scored three consecutive goals, doubling their prestige. Each goal was shot with power, unlike ordinary goals. Since China had won 7-2, they no longer sought more goals and simply managed the remaining minutes. The next match is scheduled for Saturday (the 15th). Who will win the Sino-Portuguese Cup? Let's wait for the next installment.

Saint Thomas University Basketball Team Defeats Donghua 198

Result: 43-33

Saint Thomas University Team Arrives in Shanghai Yesterday, Departing for Japan This Morning

A Group of Fifteen Will Compete in Sixteen Baseball Games in Japan

The Saint Thomas University expedition team from the Philippines arrived in Shanghai yesterday at 2 PM aboard the Russian Empress ship. They disembarked at the New Customs Wharf, where they were welcomed by Shi Zhaokang, a representative of the National Sports Association, and sports reporters from various newspapers. After landing, they went out to shop and took a short break at the Sichuan Road YMCA. At 7:30 PM that evening, they went to the Chinese Basketball Hall to compete against the Donghua basketball team. Despite the long journey and hardship, they defeated Donghua with a score of 43-33, demonstrating their strength. After finishing the basketball game last night, the team boarded the original ship and left Shanghai at 8 AM this morning, heading to Japan. They will land in Nagasaki and are scheduled to compete in sixteen baseball games in Japan before heading to Honolulu for competition and then returning to the Philippines. The detailed information is recorded as follows:

Expedition Schedule: The team of fifteen departed from Manila, Philippines, at 4 PM on April 3rd. They arrived in Hong Kong at noon on the 5th, where they competed in two basketball games and one baseball game. They left Hong Kong at noon on the 7th, arriving in Shanghai yesterday. They competed against Donghua in basketball last night and left Shanghai at 8 AM this morning, heading to Japan. They will land in Nagasaki and are scheduled to compete in sixteen baseball games in Japan before heading to Honolulu in late May or early June. They are expected to return to the Philippines around mid-July.

Team Members: The team leader is Rong Shi (Capt. DYond). The player roster is as follows: Pai Taixin, Bao De Si Tai, Na Tai'er, Santos, Ke Lie Na, Ya Xintai, Sa Balong, Bie Erba, Man De Na, Shi Tan Lusha, Bo Langte, Feng Taiweila, Ge Mubo, Xue Erfan. A total of fifteen people.

Baseball Strength: The team's goal is to compete in baseball in Japan and Honolulu. Basketball is just a warm-up act. Their baseball strength is very strong, with many members from the previous Far Eastern Games. This time, they are newly crowned champions of the three major universities and runners-up in the All-Philippines professional baseball league.

Basketball Strength: Although basketball is their warm-up act, their strength is also very strong. They are also champions of the three major university basketball leagues in Manila and winners of the Manila Basketball Championship organized by the Philippine Amateur Athletic Association. They are tied with the Alenio team. Because the competition was divided into two divisions, they and the Alenio each won one division, but the final has not been decided. Xue Erfan, Ge Gou, Man De Na, and Ya Xintai, who played last night, are all official members of the championship team.

Record in Hong Kong: After arriving in Hong Kong, the team competed against the South China team, the Hong Kong basketball champion, at the YMCA. The team won 42-28. The next day, they competed against the Hong Kong basketball runner-up, and the team won 58-42. In baseball, they played against the South China Club, winning 12-3.

Basketball Victory Over Donghua Last Night 199

After arriving in Shanghai from Hong Kong yesterday, the team went to the Chinese Basketball Hall at 7:30 PM to compete against the Donghua basketball team, formerly known as the Shanghai University team. News of the game spread, and basketball enthusiasts flocked to the event, filling the basketball hall to the brim. The scene was even more grand than the All-Nations Basketball Finals. The Philippine team's skills were extraordinary. They ran like hungry tigers pouncing on food and jumped like soaring birds. Their agility and quickness were amazing. Their work under the basket was particularly effective, passing and shooting from the crowd in an unpredictable manner. The Donghua team, formerly the Shanghai University team, plus the veteran Lu Zhongen, had improved significantly. Their performance was also excellent. However, in comparison, they were no match for the Philippine team. The Philippine team was strong and tough. Although Donghua once tied the score, the team was not discouraged. They had a plan and seemed confident of victory. Therefore, in the end, the Philippine team won 43-33. The referees were Zhang Guoxun and Li Zuqi.

Equal Start: Under the bright lights and cheers of the ladies, the two teams began their attack. Donghua took the lead, with Feng Nianhua and Qian Jingzhu scoring two consecutive goals, creating a strong momentum. The Philippine team displayed their skills, demonstrating the beauty of passing and attacking, earning applause from the audience, who marveled at the spectacle. However, the court was not heated, and the shots were often not satisfactory, so they had to temporarily concede. Donghua took the lead with 7-3, but by the end of the first quarter, the Philippine team managed to tie the score at 9-9.

Philippine Team Takes the Lead: After a short break, the game continued. Feng Nianhua scored again, taking the lead once more. But as the saying goes, "The weather is unpredictable, and people have unexpected misfortunes." Wu Guolin suddenly injured his foot and had to retire, replaced by Lu Zhongen. Lu Zhongen switched to center, and the lineup inevitably loosened. The Philippine team launched a fierce attack, with Ge Mubo scoring three consecutive goals and Pai Taixin adding two points, suddenly surpassing Donghua 17-13. At this time, Wu Guolin, whose foot had recovered, re-entered the court, facing the challenge. Lu Zhongen and Qian Jingzhu added two goals, while the Philippine team scored another five points. At the end of the first half, the Philippine team had 22 points, and Donghua had 17 points.

Intense Battle: Switching sides and continuing the game, the Philippine team replaced their center and left forward. After Ge Mubo scored two goals, Donghua suddenly gained momentum. Sun Maiqing scored two consecutive free throws, and Feng Nianhua added three points, suddenly making the score 24-26. Donghua seemed to have found life in a desperate situation, and their spirits were high. The audience also became more excited, thinking that they could make a comeback and regain their pride. However, the performance in this quarter was greatly reduced. The lineups of both sides were scattered, and the actions became too rash and fierce amidst the intense sounds, lacking the previous clarity and beauty.

Final Victory: In the last quarter, the Philippine team still used the official lineup from the first half. Donghua desperately sought victory and launched a fierce counterattack. The Philippine team was unwilling to show weakness and responded with eye contact, competing with each other, each refusing to yield. They fought so hard that everyone was panting and sweating like rain. The Philippine team was able to respond everywhere, and once again took the lead with 33-27. After Donghua's Qian Jingzhu scored, Feng Nianhua made two long shots, and everyone was spirited and full of enthusiasm. Lu Zhongen scored another free throw, suddenly making the score 33-33, with no clear winner. At this point, Donghua thought they could secure victory, but the Philippine team did not panic. Xu Tu Hongzhan, Xue Erfan scored four consecutive goals, Ya Xintai added one, and in an instant, they scored ten consecutive points. Donghua then lost the game, with the score being 33-43.

A Bird's-Eye View of Shanghai's Medical and Pharmaceutical Industry in the Past Decade (Continued) 201

— Pang Jingzhou

Chapter 4: Business Conditions

In addition to general modern doctors, let's talk about the business of members of the so-called Western Medical Association. Their business skills are often very good, their publicity is strong, and their fees are very economical, so their business is also very busy. To be fair, some of them are quite skilled at giving injections. Other than that, there is no apparent difference between their outpatient and home visits and those of other doctors, except for a few true characteristics: (A) Members of the Western Medical Association are quite capable of prescribing old-fashioned decoctions; (B) There are no formal hospitals run by members of the Western Medical Association in Shanghai, nor are there any members of the association serving as chief physicians in any public or private hospitals; (C) The association has no publications, nor are there any papers written by members of the association; (D) Members of the association who claim to be specialists are mostly in venereal diseases, and some claim to be specialists in leukorrhea, while other specialties are rarely seen; (E) No members of the association serve as professors in medical schools and teach Western medicine. Therefore, it can be said that members of the Western Medical Association are not restricted in their business compared to other modern doctors, but there are some differences in their background and level of knowledge. This phenomenon is prone to occur in the transitional era of any country and should be remedied by the government, society, and the medical community itself, rather than being completely dismissed. It is hoped that members of the Western Medical Association will also recognize this path in order to have hope of improving Chinese medicine. If you think that my chatter today is intentionally demeaning the members of the association, then there is nothing I can do. There is also a chapter on medical administration below, which describes the clues in more detail. If you read it calmly, you will understand. (B) The Business of the New Pharmaceutical Industry

As for the business of the new pharmaceutical industry, it was very undeveloped more than 30 years ago. In addition to the pharmacies opened by foreigners, which were exclusively for foreign nationals and foreign doctors, the number of pharmacies run by Chinese was very small. Zhongxi, Zhongying, and several other companies were already very old brands. At that time, because the number of modern doctors was not large, some people prescribed and dispensed medicine themselves, so the only business of each pharmacy was to sell European and American tested medicines (now called over-the-counter drugs) and also sell cosmetics, perfumes, and foreign goods. To this day, pharmacies in the interior still sell towels and umbrellas, which is the tradition of that time. Later, some pharmacies promoted their own over-the-counter drugs on a large scale and used publicity methods, which aroused the suspicion of countless people. Huang Chujiu's Sino-French Pharmacy produced Ailuo Brain Tonic, which earned him the nickname "sly." In fact, Ailuo Brain Tonic was just a foreign over-the-counter drug manufactured in China. Huang only used the psychology of the Chinese people's worship of foreigners, using more Western names and adding some Western colors, without other deceptive acts. However, to this day, how many speculative drug dealers are there on the market? How many deceptive drugs are there on the market? On the contrary, I have never heard of a third or fourth sly person coming out of Shanghai. This situation can prove on the one hand that the world is not as good as it used to be; on the other hand, it can prove that foreign science is developing day by day, while the scientific knowledge of our people cannot keep up, so the ability of society to distinguish between right and wrong is becoming weaker and weaker, which is really heartbreaking. In the past decade, due to the increase and progress of modern doctors, the new pharmaceutical industry has naturally expanded as well. The added categories are dispensing merchants, drug dealers, over-the-counter drug merchants, and pharmaceutical factories. The improved category is that dispensing merchants have gradually moved from apprentice workers to experts and academics, and all pharmacies have pharmacists. Drug dealers have also changed from selling foreign general merchandise to specializing in pharmaceuticals.

Reasons for Difficulty in Curing Gonorrhea and Correct Treatment Methods (Part 2) 202

— Liu Yunshou

(4) Everything else: There are many other reasons. First, the patient waits for the acute symptoms of gonorrhea to pass and it becomes chronic. Because there is no pain, they are unwilling to continue treatment to eradicate the disease. Second, the patient does not understand the way to maintain health (see my book "Sexual Disease Pointer" sold by Datong Bookstore). Third, there is the economic problem of not being able to seek medical treatment for a long time. Fourth, there is the occupational relationship, which makes it inconvenient to seek medical treatment. Fifth, the couple cannot seek medical treatment at the same time, resulting in a situation of mutual infection. Sixth, there is the reason for trusting all improper treatments, which leads to prolonging the time to cure.

The above has explained the reasons why gonorrhea is difficult to cure and the advantages and disadvantages of all treatments. Then, how do we find the most correct treatment method? Now I will record it item by item below:

(1) Abortive therapy: The earlier gonorrhea is treated, the more effective it is. It is best to inject a bactericidal drug into the urethra within one or two days of gonorrhea infection (that is, one or two days after unclean intercourse), before there are any conscious symptoms or pus discharge. It can be cured in just a few days. This is called abortive therapy. However, most patients who come to the doctor for treatment already have pain and a large amount of pus discharge. At this time, the gonococci on the urethra are not only on the mucous membrane, but have already invaded the tissues under the mucous membrane. If they can be treated in an orderly manner, it is not difficult to cure gonorrhea.

(2) Local treatment: Gonococci are in the urethra, so washing and dripping medicine into the urethra is naturally the most important thing. Although there are many drugs that can be used, in principle, when there are gonococci, bactericides should be used, and when the gonococci are eliminated and the inflammation has not subsided, astringents should be used. At the same time, it is necessary to observe the patient's condition and the nature of the urine, and the type of drug, the number of injections, the amount of injection, the concentration, and the time of staying in the urethra should be adjusted accordingly. There is no fixed procedure. The length of treatment depends entirely on the doctor's use of drug methods. Often, if the gonococci have been eliminated and a strong bactericide is injected again, or if there are many gonococci and a mild drug is used, not only will it not be effective, but it will increase the disease or prolong the time to cure. Therefore, it is necessary to use a microscope to check the gonococci and observe the changes in the urine. This is the standard for selecting the type and dosage of drugs and everything else.

Also, the injected drugs should not only kill the gonococci on the surface of the urethral mucosa, but also kill the gonococci lurking in various glands or collateral tubules (described later).

In chronic gonorrhea, the urethral tissue has been infiltrated. Even if drugs are injected daily, it is still not effective. At that time, other methods must be found to make the drug easily enter.

(3) Injection method: Such as the use of yellow pigment vaccine, etc., are all auxiliary methods for treating gonorrhea.

(4) Urethroscopy examination: Understanding the nature of the urethral tissue mentioned above, we can know that gonococci are easy to lurk in the urethral collateral tubules, Littre's glands, and other parts. The reason why gonorrhea recurs later due to drinking, fatigue, or intercourse is due to this. Therefore, when the urethritis has been roughly cured, or when it is chronic and difficult to cure, is it not an important thing to use a urethroscope to check the lesions of gonorrhea (lesions are the nests of pathogens)?

(5) Surgical treatment: Since there are lesions in the urethra, which are the basis for the recurrence of gonorrhea, after checking with a urethroscope, use a small sharp knife to cut it open to break the lesions, or drip medicine.

(6) "Buqi" therapy: "Buqi" is a metal curved rod made in various sizes. After urethral surgery, the wound is healed, and the "Buqi" is inserted to stretch the wrinkles in the urethra, and the injected medicine can reach the entire mucosal surface and the inside of the collateral tubule sinus glands. Moreover, the stimulation of the "Buqi" improves the blood circulation of the urethral tissue and produces healthy epithelium. Before and after gonorrhea treatment, the application of "Buqi" is also very important. (7) Oral medicine: Although there is no specific medicine for oral medicine, it can also help a lot. What medicine to use can only be adapted to the circumstances.

(8) Malaria treatment: Now there is a malaria treatment for stubborn gonorrhea, but there are not many test results and the application is not widespread.

(9) Prostate: The prostate gland is often the nest of gonococci. Prostate examination and treatment is also very important.

Observations on the Current State of Medicine (Part 2) 203

— Ji Jilin

As for why new medicine cannot fully gain the trust of the general public, there are several reasons. First, our people have always had a kind of self-sufficient mentality. Things and knowledge imported from abroad, regardless of whether they are good or bad, are regarded as foreign studies. Not only do we not learn from them, but we also absolutely attack and reject them. For example, Western machine industry is indeed better than China's, but the general public is always unwilling to wholeheartedly say, "We are really not as good as them." Instead, they insist on saying, "Although their material civilization is better than ours, our spiritual civilization seems to be better than theirs." Medicine is also like this; many people know that Western medicine is better than traditional Chinese medicine, but they are still unwilling to admit defeat, saying: "Western medicine focuses on substantial research, while Chinese medicine focuses on spiritual observation. Western medicine is certainly better than Chinese medicine in surgery, but it is far inferior to Chinese medicine in internal medicine." This is the first point. Second, the nature of our people is conservative and restorationist. The phenomenon since the Enlightenment is still the same phenomenon today. Medicine is certainly no exception; the Huangdi Neijing (Huangdi's Internal Classic) of thousands of years ago is still popular today. How Western medicine has improved and developed has not been noticed at all. It is considered that our responsibility is completed as long as we conserve our inherent medicine. Recently, traditional Chinese medicine, which calls for preserving national essence (?), can enable our country's declining medicine to gain the advocacy and approval of a part of the people, because their arguments are in line with the unique conservative and restorationist mentality of our people. The failure of Western medicine to become popular is also a great obstacle. This is the second point. Third, since traditional Chinese medicine has been in society for so many years, the general public knows a little about medical terms related to traditional Chinese medicine; for example, when we ask about their illness, they say that my liver fire is too strong, or that my kidney water is greatly deficient. There are also very profound terms such as blood heat and yin cold, which are constantly spoken out. This kind of situation is always encountered by newly qualified doctors; if they are told that their disease is gastritis or neurasthenia, they will definitely not believe it. As for medicines, many of the medicines in the prescriptions prescribed by traditional Chinese medicine are known to them to some extent; while in new medicine, except for a few common advertised medicines such as Zilai Xuetan pills, the general public has no knowledge at all; they already have a skeptical attitude towards new medicine, and at the same time they are asked to take medicines that they don't understand, so how can this arouse their faith? This is the third point. Fourth, the price of Western medicine is too high. On the one hand, because many Western medicines cannot be manufactured in China and are imported from abroad, the price is naturally more expensive; on the other hand, there are many unscrupulous people in new medicine who are too欺人 too甚 (oppressive) He knows that the society does not know the price of Western medicine, and sometimes he arbitrarily rip off the customers. This is still the medicine aspect. As for the consultation fee, the Chinese and Western medicine in big cities is of course almost the same, but the new doctors in small cities

Page 18

The cost of home visits is often several times higher than that of traditional Chinese medicine. How can people not be discouraged? In the era of the 20th century, people who are stirred up by the new trend must embrace the purpose of reforming the era. The evolution of mankind from the savage era to the civilized era is the result of continuous reform; if we only stick to the old phenomena, isn't it still a savage era? Therefore, I am extremely opposed to traditional Chinese medicine, which is outdated and does not know how to improve, but what methods can be used to gradually popularize new medicine with a spirit of improvement and adaptation to the trend in the society? First, I hope that our country should have its own manufactured medicines, and not rely on foreign supply; on the one hand, it can make up for a big leak; on the other hand, the price can be low, so that ordinary people will not dare to ask for advice because the medicine is expensive. Second, the government should strictly register traditional Chinese medicine; as for the scholarly school that kills people with ancient prescriptions, the quack school that talks nonsense, and the drug store buddy school that is neither donkey nor horse, they should all be severely cracked down on. Third, set up more public hospitals so that the general public can get the opportunity to see a doctor. Finally, I have a word to advise all new doctors. If you want scientific new medicine to be popularized in the society, you must first take the responsibility of reforming medicine, step by step forward from the dark road, and strive to eliminate all obstacles. Second, we must respect the inherent morality of doctors and arouse the faith of the general public. Third, we must truly unite with the people and make new medicine become the medicine of the public.

Scientific Guide to Safe Childbirth (12) 204

— Yu Songyun

(C) Common Sense and Key Points During Childbirth

(1) Bowel and Bladder Movements After the Onset of Labor Pains

When labor pains recur, that is, at the beginning of labor, whether or not there has been a bowel movement, an enema must be performed first, and urination should be done from time to time.

Because of the force exerted during bowel movements, there is a risk of ruptured membranes. A bedpan should be used and can be done in bed. In the early stages of labor, urination can be done at the discretion of the parturient. It is okay to go to the toilet. If the cervix has opened to three centimeters, she should be ordered to lie on her back to urinate. If urination is difficult, a urinary catheter can be used.

Why should we pay so much attention to bowel and bladder movements? Because the accumulation of bowel and bladder movements can easily induce weak labor pains, which hinders the progress of labor, so it should not be neglected.

(2) Getting Up and Moving Around

When the labor pains are not severe, the parturient can get up and move around at will. First-time mothers may as well take a walk indoors.

If the cervix has dilated to three centimeters, she must be ordered to lie down, because sitting up at this time may cause premature rupture of membranes: there is a risk of prolapse of the upper limbs or umbilical cord.

If a multipara has had a rapid labor history in the past, or has a suspended fetus, or has a history of bleeding, then; at the beginning of labor, she must be ordered to lie on her back to prevent accidents.

Young women, at their first delivery, or impatient multiparas, if they cannot restrain their fear, resulting in terror, irritability, and extreme anxiety, then; they should be advised from the side and explained as much as possible. It can be said; that childbirth is a natural physiological process and there is no danger, so you can rest assured and don't worry. If fear is unsettling, then it is dangerous instead.

Sometimes, during the dilation phase, the labor pains gradually weaken or even stop completely. If the parturient wants to sleep, and there are no other concerns, she may as well be allowed to sleep peacefully, so as to rest, wait for her to wake up once, and she can recover her energy, add strength, and then start strong labor pains again.

(3) Pushing Too Early

The parturient often uses abdominal pressure during the dilation phase. This is not only harmful but also useless, and it can easily make the parturient tired, and it can also easily cause weak labor pains. It can also cause early rupture of membranes or spastic labor pains. As a result, the progress of labor is delayed and the pain is increased instead. Therefore, at the beginning of labor, early pushing (abdominal pressure) is strictly prohibited.

(4) Diet

The parturient often does not want to eat because of the labor pains, but there are also many people who want to eat. If it is predicted that the labor process may be prolonged, it is okay to give a small amount of food, but avoid too much, such as: thin porridge, lotus root starch, egg, milk, soup, bread, etc. The drink is clear tea, clean water, avoid strong tea, coffee and alcohol. If you are tired, you can use a little wine.

The Aesthetics and Scientific Protection of Breasts (Part 2) 205

The Breast Band is the Protection of Beautiful Form

Among the various methods of protecting the position and shape of the breasts, the most necessary is to use a breast band that is suitable for oneself. Although there are ready-made breast bands sold in Western countries, because they are all the same style, of course, there is no reason why everyone can wear them flat and suitable. Breast bands that are not flat and suitable are useless. On the one hand, the breast band does not allow clothes to rub and stimulate the breasts: on the other hand, it fixes the breasts on the chest, that is, even when the body is moving, there will be no unnecessary and unpleasant shaking: especially it can prevent sagging. When walking slowly, walking fast, jumping, and bending over, if the breasts shake, this is not only unsightly, but also pulls the breast's attachment tissues, and it will feel painful.

What Style of Breast Band is Appropriate

To protect beautiful breasts; to cover up breasts that have already sagged, so as not to be ugly, and to sag even more; then a well-fitting breast band is necessary. The breast band is made of strong, loose and elastic cloth, and the lower edge is inlaid with rubber, so that breathing and upper limb movement will not feel difficult. The straps hanging on the shoulders should not be too narrow to avoid embedding in the flesh. Because the breasts will swell a little during menstruation, they should be made so that they can be tightened and loosened for adjustment.

Corset and Corslet

For fat, sagging breasts, ordinary breast bands are not suitable. Pressing heavy breasts on the chest: makes breathing difficult; and the straps also have to be embedded in the shoulders; so it is harmful instead. A Corset (belly band) must be used to support it from below. However, old-fashioned Corsets, which squeeze up the breasts and make the ugliness even more obvious, cannot be used: it is best to use a Corslet (longer vest) recently, which tightens the chest and abdomen together.

The Disadvantages of Sagging Breasts

Severely sagging breasts are not only unsightly and inconvenient for work, but also harmful to health. Obese women, because of this kind of fatty breast, the body increases even more, movement is not free, and it presses the chest: hinders breathing; harms the heart's activity; causes back pain; eczema is easy to grow under the breasts and ulcerate.

The History of Breast Cutting

Breast cutting, in ancient times, was a punishment inflicted on women. In the 194th chapter of the Code of Hammurabi, the king of Babylon in 2250 BC, it can also be clearly seen. Female warriors often cut off their right breasts in their youth in order to make the movement of their right arms free, especially to facilitate throwing stones. There were also those who burned both breasts as children in order to adapt to weapons. Some sects cut off the breasts of women serving the gods in order to prevent sexual stimulation from being spread by the breasts.

The Creation of Breast Beauty and Modern Medical Techniques

A part of modern women, in order to increase their physical beauty, fervently demanded breast cutting; and the popular style in 1932 was thin and slender, so women who sell physical beauty; women who felt that large breasts were inconvenient in their professions; and even women of the leisured class who did not want to lag behind; all excused themselves on the grounds that they were harmful to health and asked for plastic surgery, so the doctor's scalpel was placed on the breasts. Modern medical technology is advanced, so it is possible not to cut off the breasts, on the one hand, to maintain its function, and on the other hand, to cut off excess fat and delayed skin, and change it to a suitable position, beautiful and even shape. Inverted nipples are not only unsightly in form, but also difficult to breastfeed, so now there is plastic surgery to make the nipples protrude.

(This article is translated from the Popular Medicine, Volume 11, No. 12, published by the Japanese Popular Medicine Society on January 15 this year)

Several Important Discoveries and Inventions in the Development of New Medicine (3) 206

— Gu Shoubai

In addition to general anesthetics, the rest are local anesthetics.

There are also two kinds of local anesthetics. The first is cryoanesthesia. Because a part of the body is frozen, it can completely lose consciousness. This cryoanesthesia method was first created by J. Arnott in 1848. At that time, he only used a mixture of ice and snow. Although this mixture can also be used, it may not always be effective. In 1866, Sir Benjamin Ward Richardson invented a more convenient method. He used a special atomizer to spray extremely pure alcohol essence into a fine mist towards the local area. At this time, the alcohol essence evaporates extremely quickly, and it takes away a lot of warmth from this local area, making the skin freeze, turn white and harden. This cryoanesthesia method is still used today. However, because ethyl chloride can make tissues freeze faster, it is often used to replace alcohol essence.

Another local anesthesia method is to use a certain drug to paralyze the local nerves. "Cocaine" was the first of these drugs to be adopted by the medical community in 1884. In recent years, there have been many improved preparations, such as "Novocaine" and "Eucaine", which are more effective and more widely used than "Cocaine". These drugs are made into solutions of appropriate concentration and injected into the skin. After two or three minutes, this local area can lose consciousness. When these drugs are applied to the mucous membranes of the mouth, throat and nasal cavity, and inside the eye, as long as they are applied to the surface, there is no need for injection, and they already have the effect of paralyzing consciousness.

Recently, there is also a spinal anesthesia method. As long as a solution of anesthetic drugs such as "Cocaine" is injected under the spinal membrane in the lumbar canal, the nerves in the lower half of the body can completely lose consciousness. At this time, although the patient is awake, he does not feel the pain of the operation at all. For example, most hemorrhoidectomies have recently adopted this spinal anesthesia method. There is also rectal anesthesia, which has only recently been successfully tested. Although some people used liquid or vaporous alcohol essence to inject into the rectum in the past, trying to perform general anesthesia, the results all failed. In 1926, Butzengeiger used "Avertin" for rectal anesthesia. The following year, he published the results in detail. After that, many German surgeons used this method to perform surgery. This rectal anesthesia method can be used for operations on the head, neck, especially struma, Basedow's disease, and operations on the thorax and spine; however, there seem to be many objections to the application of this anesthesia method to visceral surgery.

(2) Antiseptic Sterilization Method

The main reason for the great progress of foreign science in the 19th century, in addition to the invention of the use of anesthetics, is also closely related to the invention of antiseptic sterilization methods.

In the past, suppuration of wounds was considered to be the result of contact between putrid air and the wound. Later, it was discovered that this observation was wrong. Experiments proved that there were germs in the air, making the public know that the air itself was not the cause of suppuration, thus causing a great revolution in surgery. It cannot be said that this was not the credit of Joseph Lister. Now let me briefly record the process of Lister's invention of the antiseptic method.

Lister's father was a wine merchant in London, but he was very interested in making optical instruments. Later, he actually invented colorless lenses, which became a great contribution to modern scientific research. As for Lister himself, he paid close attention to Pasteur's theory that "there are microorganisms in the air that can cause various diseases, and that sepsis and pyemia are also caused by this." Therefore, he thought that if he could invent a method to kill these pathogenic microorganisms, he should be able to prevent these diseases. After that, he published articles on Pasteur's microorganism theory in magazines.

However, Lister wanted to use chemical methods to kill germs, which was different from Pasteur's method of sterilization by heating. When Lister continued his research in Glasgow Hospital, many patients died from diseases such as sepsis, pyemia, erysipelas, tetanus, and gangrene. The number of deaths from amputations was also more than 45 percent. In 1865, Lemaire of Carlisle happened to use carbolic acid for disinfection of sewers. When Lister heard this news, he also applied carbolic acid to surgery. After two years of experience, he published the results. The operations he performed using the carbolic acid disinfection method included abscesses of the spinal cord and joints, amputation of the knee joint, surgery on the chest, and fractures of the patella.

At that time, the medical community was unwilling to believe in the effectiveness of the antiseptic method advocated by Lister, and there were even quite a few people who directly opposed it. Von Liebig and Helmholtz, who opposed Pasteur's theory the most, said: Microorganisms only exist together by chance, and are not the cause of fermentation and corruption, and the suppuration of wounds is not caused by bacteria, but by the action of enzymes, partly from the body and partly from the bandage material. Their attitude towards Pasteur's theory was still like this, so of course they did not believe in Lister's antiseptic treatment, which was closely related to Pasteur's theory. Even Lister's friend Simpson of Edinburgh also stood in opposition. Spence also said that in addition to the strong stimulation of carbolic acid to wounds, the course of wounds was no different from the traditional treatment methods. In this way, until 1872, there were only a few places in England, such as Liverpool and Manchester, that adopted Lister's antiseptic method in surgery. As for London, they simply did not know that there was such a thing. From this, it is conceivable that the attitude of the medical community towards Lister's antiseptic method was cold at that time.

In order to dispel misunderstandings, Lister often published his theories and experiments in magazines and public meetings. Later, in order to completely prevent the infection of wounds, he became more determined to study, and as a result, he published the carbolic acid atomizer and the antiseptic bandage using carbolic acid in 1871. At that time, Lister's thinking was based on Pasteur's experiments; he thought that the air contained germs, so he took these germs in the air as the object of the battle. From today's point of view, the main purpose of antiseptic sterilization is to kill the germs attached to the fingers of the surgeon, surgical instruments, and the skin surface near the wound, rather than to kill the germs contained in the air; but at that time, Lister's fundamental idea was that as long as the germs entering the wound from the outside can be killed, suppuration and infection can be prevented. This policy is still unchanged even in modern times!

When Germany fought the Franco-Prussian War from 1870 to 1871, the army had adopted antiseptic treatment. In 1872, Schultze, a German military doctor stationed in Edinburgh, published many articles on Lister's antiseptic method in the German Military Medicine Journal; as a result, everyone paid attention to Lister's wound treatment method. Later, many doctors added detailed experiments and confirmed that it was effective. When Koch discovered pyogenic bacteria and knew the nature of this bacterium in 1877-1878, Lister's antiseptic method was transformed into today's aseptic method. Later, in 1886, steam sterilization replaced the disinfection of corrosive sublimate, and in 1891, the aseptic method was actually applied.

(3) The Invention of the Microscope

At the beginning of the 17th century, the invention of the microscope made it possible to know the world that could not be seen with the naked eye like the back of one's hand, which can be said to be a new era in academics. This is as important as the invention of the telescope promoting the progress of astronomy.

Using Traditional Chinese Medicine in a Western Way (Continued) 207

— Zhou Mengbai

(10) Camphor

Origin

This product is a dextrorotatory ketone obtained from the camphor tree (CiunamomrmCamphora (LInne) NeesetEbermaier) of the Lauraceae family. The tree is an evergreen tree, more than ten feet tall. There are many yields in the eastern part of Fujian and Zhejiang. It takes decades for it to become shade. Unfortunately, in recent years, Chinese people do not know how to cherish it. It is often deeply mined and felled by the Japanese, and they do not know how to add plants. The trees have been reduced a lot.

Properties

This product is a colorless, translucent or white crystalline flexible block, or a white crystalline powder. It has a peculiar odor, with permiating qualities, a slightly bitter taste, initially pungent and hot, and then cool. One part of this product needs 800 parts of water to dissolve, but it is easily soluble in alcohol and ether.

Experiment

Add 1 gram of this product to 10 cc of petroleum benzine or 10 cc of alcohol, it should dissolve clearly and transparently. If there are insoluble substances, it means that it is mixed with paraffin and stearic acid. Also, take a copper wire and curl it into a spiral, place it in a colorless flame to burn. After the flame does not appear green, dip a small amount of this product, burn it in the outer flame first, and then move it to the lower edge of the colorless flame. The flame must not be dyed green. If it turns green, it is artificial camphor. Also, this product is mixed with aqueous formaldehyde, carbolic acid, menthol, thymol, pyroxylin, resorcinol, salol, etc., then it will liquefy. This should be noted in the preparation.

Effect

This product has a local irritant effect and weak antiseptic power. When absorbed, it excites the central nervous system, causing blood pressure to rise, breathing to increase, or sweating. In large quantities, it causes delirium, hallucinations, such as symptoms of epilepsy. Internal use is aimed at strengthening the heart and excitation, such as application to fever, typhoid fever, pneumonia, and drug poisoning. If it is used for emergency treatment of collapse, and treatment of chronic bronchitis and night sweats, etc., then use the injectable preparation of this product. Its external use is applied to neuralgia, rheumatism, frostbite, ulcers, etc., by applying it to the affected area, and it is also used as a repellent for insects.

(Appendix Old Saying) Pungent and hot, unblocks the sensory orifices, benefits stagnant qi, removes cholera, epigastric pain, cold damp beriberi, kills insects. Those with weak qi should use it more, then the body will be cold, the qi will be exhausted, and they will die.

Clearing the Name of the Peach Blossom 208

— Zhanlu

Spring is the season for brewing poetry; wine is the hook for fishing poetry; in this magnificent spring light, drinking wine while facing the flowers, every Chinese poet who understands prosody will be humming with enthusiasm, as if mosquitoes are rising from the tongue and flies are circling around the mouth.

However, the general poetic friends' singing of peach blossoms cannot get rid of the two traditional ideas of past poets: one is to lament its fate, such as the feeling of "peach blossoms are destined to be washed away by the flowing water," which comes with a stroke of the pen; the other is to ridicule its character, such as the feeling of "frivolous peach blossoms follow the flowing water," which also comes with a stroke of the pen. There is also the Xixi Conghua (trivial notes of Xixi) that caters to elegance, comparing peach blossoms to demons; and the blind fortune teller who details the eight characters, saying that if someone encounters peach blossom luck, they will inevitably have the danger of various sexual mania.

Flowering and falling is a certain process in the flower bushes; if you treat the falling petals in the wind and rain as a symbol of the peach blossom's poor fate, then plum blossoms, apricot blossoms, and the like are all destined to be poor. Why only say that the peach blossom is destined to be poor? Without the falling petals, how can the fruits be abundant; look back later, when the summer and autumn come, what kind of peaches, jade peaches, and honey peaches will arouse social love and be reluctant to let go; may I ask if plum blossoms and apricot blossoms can produce such sweet crystalline products and fat, moist kernels? The fate of the peach blossom surpasses that of the plum blossom and apricot blossom; it is not destined to be poor, then drifting with the water is not a symbol of its frivolity. The Xixi Conghua takes the peach blossom as a demon, which is especially nonsense, and it is true that the one who calls it a demon will be called a demon. The peach blossom luck in the mouth of the blind fortune teller is something that people are unwilling to accept; in fact, it is not necessarily impossible to have peach blossom luck, leaving good seeds among people, what's wrong with that?

The peach blossoms bloomed too late this year. This "Clearing the Name of the Peach Blossom" is a miscellany that I wrote when I could not see the peach blossoms during the Qingming Festival,

Fourth Company Commander of the Northeast 212

Chapter Four: The Affectionate Game Begins Again in the Teahouse, Hard Times at the End of the Year, The Pawnshop Cries in Woe

Guizhi said: "Is it always eighty or a hundred a month?" Jiang said: "If a person has this much money, it is enough to support a family." Guizhi still did not speak. Jiang said: "The old man said last time that he wanted to find a family for Company Commander Zhao. It's just that it's not easy to choose the right person. Actually..." She hesitated for a while at this point, and then continued: "A company commander who is not very old, has a good temper, and has no one at home, what other person would not want such a marriage?" Guizhi hugged the clothes in her arms,揉made them into a cloth ball, stepped down to the ground, poured a cup of hot tea with the hot water on the stove, looked at the things on the table, touched them, for about five or six minutes, and then returned to the kang to work. Jiang saw that the girl seemed unwilling to listen to such words, so she did not dare to decide whether she was unwilling to listen to such words. After a while, she slowly smiled and said: "Company Commander Zhao is a good person in every way. What do you think?" Jiang was not sure about the girl's attitude towards Zhao Ziqiang, so she simply asked the girl directly. Guizhi felt that, judging from Zhao Ziqiang's character, she really could not say anything bad about him. Her mother had eaten the person's cooked beef, and she had to compliment him a few times, so she really had nothing to say. So she replied faintly: "He's not bad." Jiang thought that the girl naturally did not want to directly say that he was good. The four words "not bad" described the girl's attitude of wanting to say good but being too embarrassed to say good. After a pause, she smiled and said: "I mean, I want to be a matchmaker for him." Guizhi, seeing her mother's attitude and hearing her words tonight, knew that there was definitely something going on. She thought to herself that ignoring her mother would be fine. Now that her mother had directly said that she wanted to be a matchmaker, this made it difficult for her to deal with. Should she deny it? Her mother was talking about being a matchmaker, not about arranging a marriage. If she expressed her unwillingness, it would seem that she was overthinking things. Should she not deny it? On the other hand, it would be considered an admission, and that would not do. It was difficult to express her attitude, and she had to express it, which was very painful. Because of the pain, she pondered for a long time and could not speak. (37)

Putting his face close to her cheeks, smelling the fragrance, and leaning against her body, he smiled obsequiously and said: "Good sister, give me the rouge on your lips to eat." While sticking to her like taffy. How fragrant and amorous, but also how cheesy! In fact, what's so objectionable about it compared to the public kissing scenes on the screen now?

Rural Figures

— Zhu Shoutong

The sky had just turned white, and the roosters had not yet sung the short song to urge people to get up. The vegetable vendor was already wearing the waning moon, stepping on the dewy fields, diligently digging up green vegetables and putting them into the carrying poles.

Although his head was covered with white hair and his forehead was deeply etched with wrinkles, he did not show any signs of aging and was still full of youthful vitality. After working for a while, he felt a little feverish, so he took off his jacket. At that time, the corners of his forehead, which were moistened with sweat, were already shining.

Shouldering the full load of vegetables, he hurried to the market with his blue-veined feet. He thought to himself: there is not much rice left in the rice jar; yesterday, the neighbor next door sent a basket of green plums, so he had to send some gifts in return; the weather is getting hot, and Ah Gou needs to add one or two pieces of coarse cloth clothing... Then he thought of Mrs. Huang, who often bought his vegetables, who was also very kind. When he saw her today, he would ask her for a few pairs of broken shoes. In front of them, a young man in a suit holding a bunch of Western newspapers saw him and hurriedly stood up, vacating his original seat. At the same time, he stretched out his free hand, raised his palm to the lady, and touched the lady's clothes with his fingers. He casually shifted his gaze and glanced at the old woman who had mistakenly taken a step forward. The lady had just sat down halfway on her buttocks when she seemed to notice something. She immediately stood up again, supported the old woman to sit properly with both hands, then stretched out her jade arm, pulled the rattan ring, and stood with her back to the young man in the crowd... This is a scene I saw on the Number 3 tram twenty minutes before writing this article.

Women's Paradise

Suzhou Women 213

— Ju Yun

When the words "Wu Girl" are mentioned, all Chinese people recognize Suzhou as the birthplace of beauties. It seems that melancholy and ill health, holding one's heart like Xi Shi, is a common affliction of Suzhou women. Moreover, people in the northern provinces even think that all southern girls who become prostitutes are Suzhou people. No wonder when the Feng Army went south in 1925 and stationed in Suzhou, they called every woman wearing a cheongsam on the street a "flower girl."

In fact, this concept is completely wrong, because in a degenerate society, there is hardly a port without prostitutes, but it is even more absurd to think that all southern prostitutes are Suzhou people. It is often the case that pleasure-seekers mistakenly believe that all prostitutes are Suzhou people, and the prostitutes themselves also pretend to be Suzhou people. Once, a Ningbo prostitute was asked where she was from. She said: "I am a Suzhou person." There are many, many jokes like this, but they still cannot reduce people's slanderous psychology towards Suzhou women!

I believe that Suzhou women are indeed pioneers in meeting the needs of modern women. In almost all inland counties, there are still many girls with bound feet, especially in those "remote areas." It seems that such strange phenomena can no longer be found in Suzhou. Women in the rural areas of Suzhou absolutely do not bind their feet. This custom did not start now. Throughout the era when women across the country were practicing foot-binding, rural women in Suzhou always went barefoot.

Hoeing the fields and gathering firewood in the mountains, women work as hard as men. Or, if we have visited Dengwei Tianping Mountain, we have seen many rural women carrying mountain sedan chairs, walking briskly and full of energy. Suzhou women are not showing weakness! In the city, except for a part of the daughters of wealthy families who live in secluded mansions, Suzhou women are not as shy and timid as others. Naturally, in the eyes of nineteenth-century people, it is considered frivolous for women to walk in the streets.

Let's look at the streets and alleys of Suzhou again. No matter what kind of shop – grocery store, dim sum shop – there are one or two women sitting behind the counter. Some are the daughters of the shopkeepers, and most of the others are respectfully called "Old Mother." Naturally, the lives of these women cannot be said to be thoroughly vocational for women, but they can probably be regarded as the prelude to vocational work for women.

Most Suzhou women, especially the daughters of ordinary families, are able to work hard and fulfill their duties as women. Then, Suzhou women are not considered backward in this era.

A Comfortable Little Bedroom 214

— Ju Yun

When furnishing a room, it is not advisable to have too much furniture, nor is it necessary to demand that it be luxurious. The most important thing is simplicity and cleanliness. If the furniture is properly matched, you will feel comfortable and at ease living in the room.

The smaller the room, the easier it is to furnish. Almost everyone living in the metropolis of Shanghai has few houses and many tenants. Whether it is a parlor, a multi-story building, or a small room, it can be furnished beautifully and completely.

Here is a picture of two small and comfortable single bedrooms, arranged according to the position of a multi-story building. Perhaps it can provide a reference for general female students and professional women who pay attention to interior decoration.
