Economic Supplement No. 17 Published Every Monday

The Future of Capitalism by Xie Juzeng 215

Why has capitalism, which was painstakingly built over the past few centuries, completely collapsed today? Where exactly has our production and sales system broken down? Can the past glory be restored? And if so, what methods can be used to restore it?

The world's business leaders stand before these fundamental questions, utterly at a loss. They repeatedly put forward excuses like "the gold standard," "tariff barriers," "reparations," "price stabilization," or other similar pretexts to mask their lack of consensus. They wring their helpless hands, seeking assistance from governments; meanwhile, world commerce is in chaos, causing the majority of people to suffer from hunger and cold, while the lives of the rest are constantly entangled in an unstable and insecure environment.

So, what are the governments of various countries doing in this era of unprecedented economic hardship? Politicians, like a continuous stream, are busy with meetings, seeking not the happiness of all mankind, but the interests of the part of the people they represent. Look at the British government, which has abandoned its long-admired free trade policy and begun to build tariff barriers. Yet, it still cannot avoid the burden of depression. In the United States, long trenches are being dug behind tariff barriers, ultimately forcing the President to use force to expel starving veterans, clear them from the capital, and finally compel the new President to implement emergency financial measures, declare a bank holiday, and barely weather the storm of the banking crisis; and the reefs ahead are numerous. Look at Japan, on the one hand aggressively invading our country, on the other hand countless children are starving to death because they have nothing to eat, and those who are made slaves and prostitutes are living worse than death.

Everywhere, kings are replaced by presidents, presidents by dictators; one regime follows another, but it's the same old soup with different ingredients, and in the end, the people still starve.

When future historians describe this particularly inept period of human history, to which people will they attribute all the evils caused by this chaotic state? This is truly an interesting question. Politicians? Business leaders? In any case, it will not be easy to write about the actions of the business leaders of this period. They allowed the great carriage of capitalism to race down the mountain along a precipitous cliff. The drivers—the masses—lacked the strength of unity to control the reins and guide the carriage safely forward, instead allowing their passengers—the politicians—to pull the ropes in their own directions, going south and north, each pursuing their own agenda. How could they expect the carriage not to overturn at the foot of the mountain! So, the leaders of some parts of the whole commerce tried to correct the unsteady passenger car with their bodies, and then put a stone under a wheel. But the momentum was too great, and finally, it crashed head-on, causing a major disaster.

Are we being critical of the leaders of the world's business community? Let us raise another question to answer carefully. Suppose one of the business units under their control experiences disorder, what would they do? The answer is very simple: they would begin to reorganize that unit, acting swiftly and powerfully to ensure that the unit immediately harmonizes with everything else, never allowing it to remain disordered for long, nor allowing the leader of that unit to cling to their position permanently. But if all the business units under their control are caught in a vortex of disorder, what exactly would they do? If they are unwilling to change those leaders, it is doubtful whether they will be able to overcome all difficulties and bravely reorganize the entire enterprise, so that work can return to its original smoothness and harmony. If this happened to only one unit, or a business controlled by any individual business leader in today's world, or a few units, it would certainly not be a problem. There are plenty of cases that have proven to be handled successfully. But once this chaotic and turbulent situation spreads to the entire world's business community, it becomes impossible to remedy through individual efforts. So, what are our leaders doing? Just look at the world's unemployment statistics, and that is the answer to this question. Yet, we are still under our capitalism, and we still cannot escape the control of the world's business leaders. They control the entire prosperity of the world:

All capitalist enterprises—except Russia—each control the world's raw materials. They control the factories, turning these raw materials into useful goods. At the same time, the world's transportation industry, with only a few insignificant exceptions, is organized along capitalist lines, extending to the world's financial organizations and banking systems, all of which are the same. They not only control everything, but also control the treatment of labor. In short, everything necessary for a prosperous world is in their hands. That being the case, in today's pessimistic and chaotic situation, wouldn't it be unfair to curse them? In fact, no. Precisely because everything is in their hands, they should work even harder than ever before they can handle this world's turmoil! It is their duty to understand the root cause of this difficulty and to have the full courage and boldness to solve this problem.

To give a few simple examples, in the eighty or ninety years before the European War, England could be said to have supplied manufactured goods to the whole world in exchange for raw materials, and from this trade, England and its industries built a prosperous foundation. During this period, the exchange of goods between England and other countries was very simple, but as the export of British machinery increased, other countries began to learn from them by stealth, and thus the state of world trade gradually became complex. Other nations, hiding behind tariff barriers, began to turn their raw materials into manufactured goods, initially only for consumption by their own people, but later, as production increased, they sold them to any country they could export to and profit from.

In the United States, this was particularly evident. It desperately produced various manufactured goods, and thus the new industrial leaders who were created began to seek markets. But after searching and searching, they could not find a market that had not been occupied by merchants from other countries, so the only way out was to resort to cheap goods, and thus fierce competition began between nations, which sowed the seeds of great chaos. Almost every country has become industrialized. New factories in all major countries around the world have begun to produce goods. This has become the main goal of governments, so they have begun to plan accordingly. Goods manufactured within their own country can be exported abroad and sold to various countries as much as possible; at the same time, goods from other countries are not allowed to be sold within their own country. Based on this policy, governments have erected or torn down tariff barriers, either raising them high or lowering them, with the result that the blood and sweat of the rest of the world's people are used as the price for the prosperity of a part of the people. Later, this chaotic situation became more and more obvious day by day, and the European War broke out. The world then immediately turned to the simple trade methods of the first fifty years of the eighty or ninety years before the Great War. England and most of the European countries competed to convert factories into the production of military supplies. International trade competition ceased. And the countries that were not involved in the war took the opportunity to sell almost everything that their factories could produce. As for the products of the factories of the warring countries, they were all consumed in large-scale destruction.

Finally, the Great War ended, and those countries that were not affected by the war were busy in the following years supplying goods to repair the ruins. At the same time, the warring countries also began to reorganize their factories and began to manufacture ordinary goods of peacetime. Thus, they gradually restored the same position of world trade as before the Great War, only to be compounded by the difficulties of complex international debts and the very complex financial problems of the world, but this was only one of the terrible legacies that the war left to mankind.

Anyone who has traveled around the world will understand that the goods produced by the world's factories have not exceeded the amount of human consumption. For example, in China, most of the 450 million people are extremely poor, and many goods, not to mention consumption, have not even been seen. And most of the people in India have nothing but a piece of cloth on their heads and a few grains of rice in their bowls. Even in Europe and the Americas, millions of people do not have what it takes to reach the ordinary standards of Western civilization, so that everyone feels the need to consider reducing comfort. So it is very clear that the world's factory production is far from enough to meet the needs of human comfort and happiness. In other words, today's production is still far below the limit of world population consumption. It is true that warehouses all over the world are filled with goods, and many farmers are unwilling to sell at a loss, and often destroy their harvests. But these situations are not so much an indication of overproduction, but rather the result of the collapse of capitalism's distribution system. From this, it can be seen that after capitalism built its system, it was not qualified enough to retain the various benefits that had been adapted. And the procedure that should be taken in this second step is obviously to organize the whole world in a comprehensive way.

Many articles have discussed this issue, and many reorganization plans have been proposed from time to time. But very few have been put into practice. I do not believe that mankind will sit idly by and watch civilization be destroyed, and refuse to do their best to preserve it. We only look at Russia to see what methods can be applied to the great experiment. As for whether this experiment is successful or not, that is not our goal; our goal is that the front line of capitalism still has two paths: one is to reorganize its sources and lead the world back to the road of prosperity; the other is to use several new great experiments to change the production and distribution of human needs. Whether people truly welcome trying new experiments in the whole world is still a question; but it is welcomed by most people that the leaders of capitalist enterprises work hard on reorganization on a better and better basis. In practice, such a reorganization is not impossible. The first step is that every industry in every industrial country must have an organization, so that every industry in every country has its management agency. Divide the smaller and less important industries into several departments and place them under the same management. At the same time, put the banking finance and the organized labor in different departments and manage them separately and in the same way.

From among the leaders of these management agencies, representatives may be selected to form a supreme council. With this council and representatives, the country's trade can be integrated, and in cooperation with the government, a way can be found to end this chaotic situation of divergent government orders, and at the same time change the tariff policy, because this policy has destroyed so much of the world's commerce over and over again!

In some countries, the current laws may prohibit the industrial organization of the above-mentioned methods. But laws can be changed, and the power of capitalism, combined with the cooperative efforts of organized labor, can easily change any law on the statute books.

Once the industries of various countries are organized in accordance with the above-mentioned methods, a "World Industrial Alliance" can be created. This is not comparable to the current League of Nations, which has no administrative power. It can truly control world trade. It has the power to curb war, not just to persuade, but also to prevent the world's products from being used for this crazy purpose.

The world's working hours can be determined by the "World Industrial Alliance," and then the stability of world prices can be sought. In this way, one of the biggest problems at the moment will disappear invisibly. If the world's industrial leaders work together through such an alliance, then its reorganization plan may be welcomed by the Chinese people, thereby increasing the purchasing power of the 450 million people and increasing the consumption of goods in the world, which will benefit both parties. This is clearly different from the imperialist policies of the powers; the imperialist policies are not welcomed by the Chinese government and people, but a "World Industrial Alliance" has no imperialist color, so it is naturally easier to achieve results. Compared with the intervention of foreign governments, which only expands disputes, it is naturally not the same.

The above-mentioned China is only an example, and there are currently many such problems in the world that need to be solved urgently. And what we want to discuss about capitalism today is whether to create a world control mechanism that is currently lacking to solve these problems, or to return its power to new organizations? Capitalist leaders should remember well that, for example, the Communist Party is organized according to a system that can control its actions all over the world. The more advanced mankind is and the more civilized the world is, capitalism can only continue to move forward like a great development if its leaders are prepared to organize the current situation that they have created in the world. With a body like the "World Industrial Alliance," financial and monetary leaders and organized labor leaders and representatives of the business community can be brought together to discuss together. And human civilization can progress to an unlimited realm, and at the same time, the suppression of war is faster and more powerful than politicians. If the working hours of the whole world are agreed upon, then human comfort and cultivation will naturally increase as a result. And many of the current diseases of world commerce can be cured by such an organization. If the leaders of capitalism continue to pursue selfish policies and refuse to broaden their horizons and think from afar, then the replacement of capitalism by communism may not be far away!

The Maris System Bank and its Actual Situation by Wang Yutong 216

In the past, the "Banking and Trust" weekly of the Shih Shih Hsin Pao published a special issue on Maris System Banks. I, in my article "The Relationship between the Maris System Bank and Civilian Finance," repeatedly stated that it is the most necessary financial system for the current civilian economy in our country. In today's capitalist society, financial institutions have always adhered to the principle of tangible collateral. The bank's loan business is generally based on the existence and certainty of collateral. The main types of collateral are various valuable securities and real estate commodities. In recent years, due to the depression in the economic world, the market prices of various securities and real estate have fallen, and it is easy to break through the price of collateral. Therefore, banks have to quickly seek to recover their claims or require additional collateral, which puts borrowers in a more difficult position. Therefore, the Maris system abandons the tangible collateral principle and is based on personal credit, completely targeting small industrial and commercial businesses and salary earners. This system was created by the American Asar Maris. To this day, it is named after him and is called the Maris System. In 1910, when Maris was the legal advisor to the bank, he repeatedly dealt with questions about small loans. Maris, on the one hand, also noted the prevalence of usury in the country, which caused the people great suffering. He then planned to study a new program to encourage thrift among the lower classes and to provide wage earners and small business owners with credit loans. In the end, the basic principles studied by Maris were: (1) Character and earning power are the appropriate basis for granting credit. (2) Based on the above principles, the loan amount can be determined by the borrower's earning power to determine a longer repayment period. (3) Such loans must be limited to use in profitable businesses. Therefore, the principle of this system is to combine character and earning power as the best guarantee.

As for the Maris System Bank's method of raising loan funds, it issues three types of securities as circulating funds, namely: (1) Type A securities 丨丨 are a simple stock-like security, sold to general investors who aim to profit. (2) Type B securities 丨丨 are interest-bearing (usually five percent) investment securities, similar to the bank's fixed deposits. This security can be paid in installments. (3) Type C securities 丨丨 are specifically used to promote to borrowers who borrow from the bank. It is also an investment security that is paid in installments (paid off in one year). However, there is no interest.

The borrowing method of the Maris System Bank: The borrower should first be recognized by the bank's loan committee, and the bank will then order him to subscribe to Type C securities. Then the borrower will mortgage it to the bank. At the same time, the borrower will issue a promissory note for one year to the bank. The amount is the same as the Type C securities purchased, so that the amount of securities can be paid off and the loan can be paid off at the same time. Ordinary Type C securities are paid in fifty installments, once a week, and paid off within one year. The date when the payment is cleared is the time when the loan is repaid.

The Maris system is most prevalent in the Far East, especially in Japan. There are such institutions in the cities of Tokyo, Osaka, and Kobe. The most famous ones are the Japan Commercial and Industrial Promotion Corporation, the Showa Maris Commercial and Industrial Corporation, and the Osaka Maris Commercial and Industrial Corporation. The Japanese Maris

The system of financial system still takes the principle of personal credit without collateral as the principle. The most important points of decision are all based on the borrower's credit, character, and past experience. When Japan planned to implement it at the beginning, it also intended to target salary earners and small and medium-sized industrial and commercial businesses. However, because Japan's situation is different from that of the United States, the general salary earners have not been able to make full use of it. Therefore, its development center has inevitably gradually become concentrated on small and medium-sized industrial and commercial businesses. Therefore, the names of its business institutions often include such things as commerce and industry. As for the operating entity of the Maris system, it has been recognized as a formal type of banking of the Maris type in the United States. However, in Japan, any financial institution that is not regulated by the Banking Law shall not be called a bank. Therefore, the Japanese Maris System financial institutions always become institutions that run in separate ways from ordinary banks. In other words, the bank sets up another operating institution outside its own organization to handle the financial business of the Maris system. It also sets up a control agency丨HoldingCompany to handle it. The former is the administrative agency, and the latter is the legislative agency.

The increase in capital and payment of shares of the Maris System financial institutions by Japanese banks is also limited by the provisions of commercial law. It cannot be handled directly by itself, and is all handled by another control agency that is set up. And it manages the fully paid-up shares. As for the operating institution, it specializes in the business of lending. That is, when a borrower purchases securities, the control agency will also handle it.

The circulating funds of the Maris System financial institutions in Japan still hold the payment funds of the stock to offset the use. If it is necessary and the payment is insufficient, it can be borrowed separately. But this is an exception. The types of stocks are generally the following three items.

(1) Ordinary stock is the stock of an ordinary limited company. It is recruited at the beginning of its establishment and is the same as ordinary stock. When the company has no surplus, it shall not pay dividends. (2) Remuneration stock is recruited from outside with the purpose of earning profits. The funds paid for this stock are the main part of the circulating funds of the Maris System financial institutions. According to the provisions of Japanese commercial law, dividends must be paid from the surplus. However, this stock, regardless of whether the company is profitable or not, pays a fixed amount (generally five percent per year) to each stock purchaser in the name of remuneration. This is similar to the bank's ordinary fixed deposits.

(3) Installment payment stock Any person who wants to request a loan must subscribe to this installment payment stock. The shares must be paid in installments.

As for loans, they are only limited to stock purchasers. The loan applicant should first subscribe to a certain number of shares and pay the shares in installments. Then the operating institution will lend the funds according to the applicant's performance in paying the shares in installments. However, the amount is at most twice the amount subscribed by the other party. No collateral is required when borrowing. However, two guarantors should be provided. After the borrower obtains the loan, he must continue to pay for the purchased shares until the full amount is paid. Then, it will be transferred and sold to the control agency, and the funds obtained from the sale will be used to pay off the debt.

How to Solve the Unemployment Problem in Our Country by Deng Youzhi 217

After the Industrial Revolution, the mechanical industry replaced the handicraft industry, leading to a surplus of labor. This trend became serious after the war, and is even more severe today, especially in Germany. Due to the lack of statistics in our country, the number of unemployed people cannot be accurately determined. However, considering the widespread poverty in the country, it can be inferred that the number must be alarming. Nevertheless, there is a significant difference between the causes of unemployment in European and American countries and in our country. In those countries, unemployment is due to the extreme development of industry and commerce, where machines are used for mass production to replace labor, drastically reducing the demand for workers and causing unemployment. In our country, unemployment is due to the underdevelopment of industry and commerce, resulting in minimal demand for labor. Now, let's discuss only the causes of unemployment and its solutions in our country. The unemployment problem in Europe and America will be omitted.

(A) Types of Unemployed People

Unemployed people can be roughly divided into the following five categories: (1) Those who rely on ancestral inheritance and do nothing, who can be considered as non-workers. (2) Those who are unsuitable for employment due to old age or disability. (3) Those who do not have a fixed occupation, cannot maintain a living, and are frequently unemployed. (4) Those who engage in temporary occupations and cannot find another job afterward. (5) Those who lack the skills for any suitable occupation and therefore cannot be hired.

(B) Causes of Unemployment

(1) Causes related to the unemployed themselves: (1) Fundamentally lazy and enjoy the fruits of others' labor. This category accounts for the largest number in our country. Often, those with a few thousand yuan in farmland or savings become lazy and refuse to work, living at home and spending their days without engaging in production, and often indulging in excessive consumption. These people are the most shameful among the unemployed, not even as good as a lowly messenger. However, in recent years, due to the general economic decline, the exploitation by officials, and the pressure from foreign economic forces, this type of person has gradually decreased. Furthermore, the public has gradually begun to view having no occupation as shameful, which is a good sign and should continue to decline. (2) Due to the laziness, poor character, bad habits, or extravagance of the workers, they are dismissed by their employers.

(2) Causes beyond the control of the unemployed: (1) The outbreak of war or disasters causes panic in the economy, leading to unemployment. (2) The invention of new machines increases unemployment due to the adoption of new technology. This is not common in our country because we have not yet reached a stage of industrial development. (3) The economic downturn from prosperity causes panic and unemployment. (4) Seasonal changes, such as plasterers being unable to work on rainy days, and tea makers becoming unemployed after the tea season. (5) Intense competition and oversupply of the same goods cause businesses to shut down. The closure of a factory or store generates thousands or tens of thousands of unemployed people. (6) The relocation of industries from one place to another. (7) Changes in trends, such as the shift from small caps to felt hats, or from one pattern to another. During the period when consumers' preferences change, countless unemployed people can be created. (8) The cheap labor of child and female workers allows them to replace male workers, thus aggravating the unemployment problem for men.

(C) Methods of Relief

Relief methods can be divided into two types: emergency relief and fundamental relief.

(1) Emergency Relief Methods: (1) Providing the unemployed with money or goods as relief, which has a charitable nature and can only be applied in emergencies and cannot be sustained permanently. If such material assistance is given, not only will the providers be unable to sustain it, but it will also foster laziness among those receiving aid. (2) Implementing emergency public works. This is an emergency measure taken by the government to provide jobs to the unemployed to alleviate their distress. This method is more beneficial than the previous one because it promotes the goal of self-reliance among the unemployed. Examples include building dams, repairing roads, and dredging rivers. Last year, when Wuhan was flooded, the government encouraged disaster victims to build dikes as a form of work-for-relief, which belongs to this category.

(2) Fundamental Relief Methods: (1) The government should crack down on those who rely on inheritance and do nothing. These people not only fail to contribute their abilities to society but also exploit the labor of others, like social parasites. The government should crack down on them, and public opinion should condemn them. (2) Prevent population concentration and try to prohibit people from moving to densely populated cities as much as possible. (3) Promote industrial education to integrate knowledge and skills, so that everyone has a specialized skill. (4) The government should establish employment agencies to enable employers and workers to find suitable matches through the agency's introduction, thus avoiding unnecessary labor and expenses. (5) Implement a mandatory labor unemployment insurance system. It would be best if the central or provincial government could act as the insurer themselves; otherwise, the state should at least subsidize insurance companies that do not operate for profit. (6) Expand and consolidate state-owned enterprises, using machines for large-scale operations, so that labor disputes, strikes, unemployment, and other issues can be eliminated invisibly. (7) Adjust state-owned enterprises. Due to seasonal changes, the demand for labor fluctuates. The government should determine the increase and decrease in demand and use state-owned enterprises to mediate. This ensures that the supply of labor is neither excessive nor insufficient. In other words, when the general industry needs a lot of labor, suspend some non-urgent state-owned enterprises. When the labor demand decreases, resume these non-urgent state-owned enterprises to absorb a large number of unemployed people.

The relief methods are as described above. Some may argue: If our country adopts large-scale machine production, won't it repeat the mistakes of European and American countries today? I say no. Machines themselves are not only innocent but also capable of promoting work efficiency. What matters is how they are used. European and American countries have extensively applied machines to private industries, leading to the dead end of imperialism today. If we can have a virtuous, strong government with unlimited determination and ambition to use machines under the principle of state ownership, not only can we elevate this aging nation to a state of industrial development, but the unemployment problem can also be resolved.

Commercial News 218

Finance

Money Market Trading Quiet on Sunday

Yesterday, due to it being Sunday, banks were closed as usual, and there were no significant transactions in the money market to report. The interbank overnight loan rate in the market was 2%, for both silver dollars and silver. The trading of discounted drafts was also not very active, with over 3.7 million in the morning session, over 300,000 in the afternoon session, 700,000 to 800,000 in the small clearinghouse, 200,000 from out-of-town sources, and over 23 million in silver dollar drafts settled by money shops. Tongqing Exchange Shop Deposits Reach One Million

Since the Tongqing Exchange Shop on Ningbo Road began operating various deposit accounts without introductions on the 6th of this month, many people from all walks of life have been bringing money to open accounts. As of yesterday (the 9th), the total amount of these deposit accounts has reached one million, and there is a rush to continue opening accounts. Supplementary Measures for the Banking Industry 219

The Shanghai Banking Association sent a letter yesterday stating that the association held an emergency meeting today to discuss supplementary five items regarding the currency reform problem: (1) The three-bank exchange institutions will continue to operate, but will only be allowed to exchange silver taels for silver dollars, extending the time; (2) If banks and money shops receive silver checks from foreign banks, the receiving bank or money shop must endorse them and sign the statement: "(This check is only allowed to be exchanged for silver dollars at the Central, China, and Communications Banks)" before entering it into the silver dollar account; (3) Foreign banks' silver tael promissory notes must be converted into silver dollars at the legal rate of 0.715 before they can be used; (4) Promissory notes due before April 15th can be paid at a rate of 0.715 silver dollars per tael. If the due date is after April 15th and there is no issue date, they should be registered with the association before April 15th, and silver dollars will be paid at a rate of 0.715 when due; (5) All foreign exchange transactions must be settled with silver dollars. Payments for items 2, 3, 4, and 5 above will be submitted by the two associations to the Ministry of Finance for referral to the judicial authorities for record.

Securities Market Fluctuated with the Situation Last Week 220

Resulting in More Declines than Gains

Last week, from April 3rd to 8th, the Shanghai Chinese Securities Exchange was open for trading for only three days due to the Arbor Day holiday from the 3rd to the 5th. During this time, due to the market closure, the opening prices fluctuated considerably. Thursday was the first day after the holiday. Due to the sudden tension in Qinhuangdao, the resurgence of chaos, and Chairman Chiang's expedition to suppress the Communists, public confidence suddenly weakened. The Northern Faction and a certain large investor sold heavily, and retail investors followed suit, causing the market price to fall by more than one yuan. Unexpectedly, on Friday, there was a sudden reversal. Rumors of the collapse of the Japanese cabinet and a possible slowdown in the military policy boosted morale, and the market price rebounded by more than one yuan. The price movements over the two days canceled each other out. On Saturday, there were more rumors, and public sentiment turned from hot to cold again. The market price fell by one yuan again due to the emergence of large investors such as No. 38. Therefore, the weekend price was several jiao to more than one yuan lower than the previous week. Among them, Demobilization Bonds fell the most, by one yuan and two jiao. The total trading volume was 23.9705 million yuan, including 30,500 yuan in spot transactions and 23.94 million yuan in futures transactions. Among them, unified salt tax bonds accounted for over 9.1 million, demobilization bonds accounted for 3.79 million, 1929 bonds accounted for 3.9 million, 28th and 28th customs bonds accounted for 4.99 million, and the Transportation bond also traded over 1.2 million. The rest traded for tens of thousands to one or two hundred thousand.

Silk and Tea Hangzhou and Shaoxing Spring Silkworm Seed Selection Begins 224

Provincial Field Personnel are dispatched to various regions to persuade people to incubate improved varieties

Zhejiang's spring silkworms hatch earlier than those in Jiangsu, and those in Hangzhou and Shaoxing hatch more than ten days earlier than those in Huzhou. As the Qingming Festival approaches, spring silkworm farming has begun in Hangzhou and Shaoxing. Seed selection is currently underway, and the Provincial Agricultural Improvement Field is planning to send personnel to various regions to persuade farmers to cultivate improved varieties. However, it is difficult to change the local customs, and there is deep faith in local varieties such as Wangze (produced in Xinchang), Baimei (produced in Shengxian), Zhugui (produced in Zhuji), and the Yuhang variety produced in Yuhang. Many farmers still prefer to keep the methods in more remote areas, and in the Haining area, some still follow the old method of soaking local varieties in salt water for three days two days before Qingming Festival, and then transferring them to lime water for about twenty minutes before taking them out, placing them in a ventilated place to dry, and then incubating them. As a result, the sales of improved varieties produced by various manufacturing fields (commonly known as foreign varieties) are lower than last year.

(Harbin) On the 8th, the (puppet) Manchurian government ordered various agencies in Manzhouli to block eight sections of the Chinese Eastern Railway at Manzhouli Station. (Harbin) The (puppet) Manchurian government has blocked the connection between the Chinese Eastern Railway in Manzhouli and the Trans-Baikal Railway line. Russian officials of the Chinese Eastern Railway are temporarily silent. The deputy director's words have deep implications, as the Russian side has no right to protest against the (puppet) Manchurian actions. Fearing that (puppet) Manchuria will implement a blockade of the eastern border railway, it expressed this subtle diplomatic statement in order to gauge (puppet) Manchuria's opinion. 中央國府今晨之紀念週 232

陳果夫報告如何興復農村

(Nanjing) The Central Government held a memorial week this morning, with over 500 attendees, including Ye Chucang, Chen Guofu, Ju Zheng, Chu Minyi, Huang Jichen, Zhang Ji, Hong Ludong, and staff. Because Li Shizeng went to Shanghai, Chen Guofu gave a report on "How to Revive the Rural Areas." The main points were that the prices of agricultural products are now roughly three to four times higher than they were decades ago, but the lives of farmers are still very difficult, and rural areas are increasingly heading towards bankruptcy. The reason is that the prices of other goods are extremely high, so the income of farmers is not enough to cover their costs and labor. People generally say that to help the rural areas, we should start by improving seeds and increasing production, etc. In fact, the prerequisites for revitalizing the rural areas are: (1) actively carrying out water conservancy projects, (2) setting minimum prices for agricultural products to maintain the cost of farmers, (3) organizing financial institutions suitable for the needs of farmers, and (4) encouraging and assisting farmers to engage in side businesses during agricultural off-seasons. Only in this way can we save the bankruptcy of rural areas. Other industries and commerce will also prosper accordingly, and then all major plans for national salvation will be effective. Otherwise, if the rural organization collapses, the country will perish without the invasion of foreign enemies. The speech ended at 9 o'clock, and the meeting adjourned. (10th Central News Agency Dispatch)

(Nanjing) The National Government held a memorial week at 9 a.m. on the 10th, with over 400 attendees, including Yu Youren, Shao Yuanchong, Niu Yongjian, Li Yuanding, Lin Xiang, He Yaozu, Lü Chao, and National Government staff. He said that our army used their flesh and blood to resist the enemy's sophisticated equipment. Moreover, there were many mountains outside the passes, and our army built trenches in the rocks. If enemy planes bombed, the explosion of the rocks would cause extremely heavy losses. However, the morale was not weakened at all, and they were all willing to endure sacrifices in order to seek permanent survival for the nation. This spirit of sacrifice by the soldiers at the front can inspire the people of the whole country to share the same hatred for the enemy, and it will also make the international community know that our nation is not to be insulted. Its significance is extremely important. He further hoped that all military personnel in the country would be able to perform their duties and go to the front to kill the enemy, and save China through sacrifice and struggle. Prime Minister Saito and other cabinet members, the military, and the upper house are making every effort to persuade him to stay, but the results have not yet obtained Takahashi's consent. Dentsu, Tokyo, 10th - The Seiyukai, hoping to gain power, is organizing a policy investigation committee based on the policy-first principle advocated by President Suzuki over the years. This morning, it first held an association of party executives and policy investigation committee staff, and then in the afternoon, it held the first general meeting of the policy investigation committee at the headquarters hall, declaring the fundamental principles for establishing policies and investigative items. In particular, it must move towards establishing a new policy after leaving the League of Nations and banning gold exports again. When investigating, it is natural to re-examine the past policies, but in view of the objective situation of international politics and economy, it will strongly advocate establishing and expanding the national economy as the top priority. The major issues and countermeasures currently advocated by the Seiyukai's policy investigation committee are roughly as follows: (1) "Diplomatic Policy" The fundamental policy of the Empire's diplomacy has now been established. This can be clearly understood from the Imperial Rescript issued the other day. It is appropriate to follow the Holy Will, promote Japanese justice, and study appropriate and effective countermeasures. (2) "Japan-Manchukuo Control and Liaison Issues" Regarding the development of Manchukuo and the utilization of its resources and the cultivation of purchasing power, the establishment of Japan-Manchukuo unity and control is the focus, and the coexistence of the mainland industry and Manchukuo industry is sought. Regarding tariffs and other issues, careful investigation and research are conducted. (3) "Industrial Policy" After the ban on gold exports again, the changes in domestic and foreign affairs should be considered. The five-year plan of the Seiyukai previously announced should be re-examined. In particular, regarding the relationship between currency policy and fiscal policy, it is necessary to focus on smooth currency circulation. Based on this view, the Bank of Japan's actions in the market must be specially studied. (4) "Fiscal Policy" Although it is based on seeing through the future of finance and establishing a fiscal plan, it is factually impossible to eliminate the deficit immediately. Therefore, it is necessary to first establish a fiscal policy and seek harmony between finance and national defense. Based on this view, the reorganization of administrative finance must be carefully studied, and the issue of tax increases should also be considered.

Jinnensha, Tokyo, 10th - The National Alliance took the issue of Minister of Justice Oyama's retention as the starting point of the coup. After a secret meeting of President Adachi and various executives, the party headquarters decided to overthrow the current cabinet with the unity of the party. Most cabinet members below the Prime Minister hoped to stabilize the political situation by retaining the Minister of Justice, and painstakingly planned a cabinet life-saving strategy. The National Alliance considered this action to be deceiving the people, so it decided to oppose the Seiyukai's policy of gaining power and the Minseito's policy of prolonging the life of the cabinet. It will do its best to impeach the cabinet, and will start a national tour from the 16th to publicize the current cabinet's failures in order to expand the party's influence.

After repeated investigations by various parties, it was learned that he was originally a deserter who had been ordered to be arrested by the Marugame Military Police Sub-Division. His name was Mitsugi Mitsujiro. In August of Showa 4, he was a private second class in the 7th Company of the 12th Infantry Regiment in Marugame. Later, because he did not want to be dispatched to Manchuria, he secretly deserted and went to Manchuria privately to serve as a member of the Japanese volunteer army. His previous claims were completely false. He was handed over to the Takatsuki branch of the Osaka Military Police at 6 o'clock on the 5th.

It will have a commander, chief of staff, adjutant, chief engineer, chief accountant, and other key members, as well as warrant officers, non-commissioned officers, and appointed civil officials. Bai Chongxi Invites Li Jishen to Return to Guangxi 263

Guangdong Province Pays Close Attention to Li's Return to Guangxi

Li's Trip Unlikely in the Near Future

Guangzhou Correspondence: Li Jishen resigned and went south to recuperate in Hong Kong a long time ago. Some time ago, his subordinates returned to Guangdong to engage in activities, which aroused suspicion from the Guangdong authorities, leading to various rumors. Li immediately sent a letter to Chen Jitang, clarifying all the external rumors. After this matter subsided, Li remained depressed and feigned illness in Hong Kong. In Guangdong Province, those who supported Li lost power due to Li's situation over the past few months. Unexpectedly, recently, the military and political authorities in Guangxi Province suddenly expressed their intention to welcome Mr. Li back to Guangxi. It is said that the telegram from Guangxi inviting Li was jointly sent by Bai Chongxi, Deputy Commander of the Fourth Group Army, and Huang Xuchu, Chairman of the Guangxi Provincial Government, on the 24th of the previous month to Mr. Zhang Renmin, Chief of Staff of the Army, who forwarded it to Mr. Li's residence in Hong Kong. The original telegram read, "Mr. Zhang Renmin of Guangzhou, please forward this to Mr. Li Rengong, who has been in retirement for a long time. We deeply miss and admire you. Currently, internal and external troubles are pressing in, and the people's livelihood is becoming increasingly depleted. Guangxi must revive its rural economy, but construction cannot continue. Both time and economy are constrained. We, Xi and others, serve our homeland with heavy responsibilities and limited talents. We feel deeply inadequate to cope with this critical period. You have been deeply concerned about your homeland recently. We respectfully invite you to return to Yong to provide guidance. We are overjoyed and eager to see you. Please telegraph the date of your departure so that we can welcome you. Bai Chongxi and Huang Xuchu bow." It is noted that this telegram was not sent directly from Yong to Hong Kong but was telegraphed to Zhang Renmin in Guangzhou for forwarding, which seems to have a purpose. Guangxi had long intended to welcome Li, but they did not express it independently because they had not gained the sympathy of Guangdong. However, since Guangdong had rejected Li before, they would naturally pay special attention to Li's return to Guangxi. Therefore, this move has become an important issue in the Southwest. It is said that Mr. Li has not yet decided whether to return to Guangxi after receiving the telegram. Judging from the situation, it is feared that Mr. Li's return to Guangxi will not be easily realized in the near future. (April 2)

Page 22

Japan's National Census (Tokyo Correspondence) (March 31) 264

Like other countries, Japan conducts a national census every ten years, which the Japanese call the "National Census." The Japanese National Census mentioned here refers to the second Japanese National Census at the end of 1930. This is not a matter of history but a current event. In the United States, detailed reports are usually available after five years. Therefore, the National Census recently published by the Japanese Bureau of Statistics is still a general overview. However, we can also recognize the strength of our enemy to some extent. This is the only reason I want to introduce it.

(1) Total Population

As of October 1, 1930, the exact calculated population of Japan was 64,450,000. The increase rate is as follows:

Total Population Increase Compared to Previous Increase Rate

(Thousands)

1920 55,963 丨丨丨 丨丨

(Thousands)

1925 59,736 3,773 6.7

1930 64,450 4,713 7.9

The national average population density is 169 people per square kilometer. In reality, the population is never evenly distributed throughout the country and is often concentrated in several important areas. We will list the population density of various regions in Japan as follows:

Location Population Per Square Kilometer

Tokyo Prefecture 2,522 people

Osaka Prefecture 1,952 people

Kanagawa Prefecture 1,688 people

Fukuoka Prefecture 512 people

Kagawa Prefecture 394 people

Saitama Prefecture 384 people

Aichi Prefecture 505 people

The following prefectures have lower densities:

Hokkaido 32 people

Iwate Prefecture 64 people

Akita Prefecture 85 people

Aomori Prefecture 91 people

Miyazaki Prefecture 98 people

Japan's national population density of 169 people per square kilometer ranks second among the major powers, as follows:

Country Population Density

United Kingdom (Mainland) 196 people

Germany 133 people

France (Mainland) 76 people

United States 16 people

The concentration of population in cities is an inevitable phenomenon under capitalism. Now, let's compare the urban and rural population of Japan as follows:

Per Thousand People

Year Urban Population Rural Population

The increase in unmarried people is also due to the economic downturn. The lower number of unmarried women compared to men is because women marry at a younger age. The higher number of widowed women compared to men is because it is acceptable for men to remarry, while it is considered immoral for women to remarry.

(3) Occupational Distribution

In the total population, the distribution of employed and unemployed is as follows: Employed (%) Unemployed (%)

Conclusion

In general, imperialists, when a country has a small population, propagate to the public that a small population poses a risk of being invaded by other countries and strive to promote childbirth. When the population is larger, they immediately say that we have an overpopulation and must develop outward to survive. These few words lightly reveal the imperialist's aggressive mentality. The so-called overpopulation and "lifeline" are nothing more than excuses for imperialist aggression. Japan's population density of 169 people per square kilometer is far different from Belgium's 266 people per square kilometer and the United Kingdom's 196 people per square kilometer. Moreover, Hokkaido has vast land and sparse population, which can be migrated. How can there be an overpopulation? The so-called lifeline and population problem are nothing more than theories fabricated by imperialist scholars.

Guizhou Representative Zhang Yunliang Arrives in Guangdong 265

Reports to the Southwest Political Affairs Council on the Recent Situation in Guizhou Province

And Discusses the Issue of Southwest Unity in the Future

Guangzhou Correspondence: Since Wang Jialie returned to Guiyang and resumed his leadership of Guizhou's administration, his wife, Ms. Wan Shufen, was previously sent to Guangdong to discuss everything with the authorities of the Southwest Political Affairs Council. Later, the Southwest established a National Defense Committee, and Guizhou Province also sent Lu as Wang's representative to attend. Recently, there was news that You Guocai was planning to rely on the strength of Yunnan Province to return to Guizhou. Therefore, Wang Jialie specially sent Representative Zhang Yunliang to Guangxi and Guangdong to discuss all military and political liaison matters with the authorities of the two provinces. After meeting with Bai Chongxi in Guangxi, Mr. Zhang arrived in Guangzhou on the afternoon of the 2nd of this month. On the 3rd, he went to the Southwest Political Affairs Council to visit Li Zongren and various important military and political figures in Guangdong. He will travel from Guangdong to Hong Kong in the coming days to visit Hu Hanmin and discuss important official matters. According to Mr. Zhang, his mission this time is purely to report the recent military and political situation in Guizhou Province to the Southwest authorities and to discuss the issue of the Southwest's unity in the future. Since Wang Jialie took charge of the administration of Guizhou Province, he felt that most of the province's income was spent on military expenses. In order to engage in construction, he had to start with demobilization. It is reported that Guizhou Province has about twenty regiments. Since the political change, Chairman Wang decided to reduce the total number of troops in the province to ten regiments and allocate the saved military expenses to construction funds. The province's annual income is about 12 million yuan. In the past, annual military expenses reached 10 million, and there was no ability to develop construction. It is now planned to cut 10 regiments of troops, which cost about 5 million yuan in military salaries annually, leaving about 7 million yuan. 3 million yuan will be used for construction expenses, 3 million yuan for administrative expenses, and 1 million yuan for social welfare undertakings. If this plan can be implemented, the administration of Guizhou Province will be able to gradually prosper. Recently, various provinces in the Southwest are preparing to send troops to aid Rehe. Guizhou Province will also酌 (duó)編援熱軍 (zhuó biān yuán rè jūn - carefully plan and compile troops to aid Rehe) according to its capabilities. This move is being actively planned, but the military salary item is still under consideration. Chairman Wang previously planned to send me to Guangdong to serve as the director of the Guizhou 25th Army's office in Guangdong. Later, because I had other tasks, Chairman Wang sent Wang Jiezi to Guangdong to serve as the director of the Guizhou Army's office in Guangdong, so that he could contact the Guangdong military and political authorities at any time. As for the remnants of Mao You in Guizhou Province, they have now been resolved one after another. Currently, Che Yiming's troops in eastern Guizhou only have 1,000 guns and have been reorganized into a brigade, with Che still serving as the brigade commander. The remaining 300 to 400 people in You Guocai's troops in western Guizhou have all been incorporated. Jiang Bixu's troops in the north are also not a problem. All the troops in Guizhou Province are compiled into the 25th Army, with Wang Jialie serving as the army commander and Hou Tiejian serving as the deputy army commander, etc. It is also reported that the Southwest Political Affairs Council has sent Gan Jiayi to Guiyang today (the 5th) to discuss with Wang Jialie about coordinating Guizhou Province's dispatch of troops to aid Rehe. On the political side, Mr. Wang Shudu has been sent back to Guizhou to convey everything. (April 5)

Zhang Xueliang and His Family Board a Ship Tonight and Leave the Country Tomorrow Morning 266

Bade Farewell to Old Subordinates Such as Wang Shuhan at His Residence in Shanghai Last Night

Has Not Yet Decided Where to Settle After Arriving in Europe, Will Travel to Various Countries

Foreign Minister Luo Will Arrive in Shanghai This Afternoon From Beijing to See Him Off

Zhang Xueliang, the former acting chairman of the Beiping Military Council and member of the North China Political Affairs Committee, telegraphed his resignation at the beginning of last month and came to Shanghai to recuperate. Due to accumulated overwork triggering old illnesses, he sought medical treatment and has gradually recovered. He bade farewell to old subordinates at his residence in Shanghai last night. He is scheduled to board the Conte Rosso tonight with his family and leave for Italy tomorrow morning. The details are as follows:

Bidding Farewell to Old Subordinates 267

After arriving in Shanghai, Mr. Zhang was seriously ill and declined to meet with guests. After receiving medical treatment, his old illness has been completely cured, and his spirits have gradually recovered. Last night, he received more than ten old subordinates, including Wang Shuhan, Zhang Zhenlu, Liu Mingjiu, Gao Jiyi, and Liu Zhe, to say goodbye. Because he has resigned from all military and political positions, he only spoke of old friendship and the sorrow of parting. Mr. Feng Yong also visited Mr. Zhang at 11:00 this morning, talked for a long time, and then took his leave.

Boarding the Ship Tonight 268

Mr. Zhang is scheduled to board the Conte Rosso tonight and leave Shanghai for Europe tomorrow morning. Also on board are Count and Countess Ciano, the Italian Minister to China. Accompanying him are Mrs. Zhang Yu Fengzhi, his daughters Lu Ying, sons Lu Xun, Lu Ri, and a young son who is still in infancy and has not been named. In addition, there are advisor Donald, secretary Shen Zutong, and more than ten attendants.

Haven't Decided on a Place to Live 269

Reports say that Mr. Zhang will settle in Switzerland, where he has hired workers to build a house and will wander among the lakes and mountains. Reporters from the Xinsheng News Agency met at the Zhang residence and learned that Mr. and Mrs. Zhang have decided to go to Italy first and then travel to various countries. The itinerary after arriving in Italy will be decided in Europe. The only country for which a visa has been obtained is Italy. Although Mr. Zhang resigned and left the country, not asking about military or political affairs, as a citizen, he has a natural duty to both the country and the world. He will return to China soon to fulfill his duty.

Luo Arrives to See Him Off 270

According to a certain important person, Foreign Minister Luo Wen'gan has been in Shanghai for three days to see off Mr. Zhang and the Italian Minister. He is staying at the Cangzhou Hotel. However, after various investigations, it has not been confirmed that Mr. Luo has indeed arrived in Shanghai. However, according to reliable sources, Mr. Luo will arrive in Shanghai this afternoon, which means that it is a fact that Mr. Luo came to Shanghai to see off Mr. Zhang.

Pre-Departure Statement 271

In addition, Ning Wu, as Mr. Zhang's representative, answered the reporter's questions as follows: (Question) Does Deputy Commander Zhang have any statement before leaving the country? (Answer) Commander Zhang himself is now very willing to meet with you, but due to the doctor's instructions, he refuses to meet with guests and talk. However, Commander Zhang has repeatedly stated that the general situation of his departure from the country has been expressed in past telegrams. Therefore, he cannot comment on political issues for the time being because he is out of office. However, as a citizen, he will still devote himself to the party and the country after returning from his inspection. The inspection period is scheduled for six months. In addition to the military and political situation during his years of service, he will also pay attention to social undertakings. This trip will first go to Italy, and he plans to stay longer. Whether to go to Germany or the United States will be decided after arriving in Italy. (Question) Regarding the Beijing telegram about the antiques and calligraphy in the Summer Palace being taken away by Commander Zhang, has Mr. Zhang heard the details of this matter? (Answer) I have also seen this news, but I do not know the details. However, judging from what I have known about Commander Zhang's following over the years, this fact is not accurate. The calligraphy and paintings in the Summer Palace are under the jurisdiction of the Beijing Municipal Government. Even if Commander Zhang borrowed them for viewing, he would definitely return them. Commander Zhang did not have this kind of situation when he was in power in the past, and he will not have this kind of thing now that he is out of office. He obeyed the Central Government's orders in everything. This time, he obeyed the Central Government's orders and handed over hundreds of thousands of troops to the Central Government. From this, it can be seen that he is very clear between public and private matters. (Question) What about the sale of the Tianjin Naval Hospital? (Answer) Deputy Commander Zhang has absolutely stated that he has not heard of this matter and does not know where it came from. (Question) Has Chairman Chiang recently exchanged telegrams? (Answer) Chairman Chiang has sent letters repeatedly, but they only concern private matters and do not involve politics. Minister Song often visits him. (Question) What is the condition of Mr. Zhang's illness? (Answer) He is deficient in both qi and blood and is only receiving treatment.

Shen Jinding Discusses that European Countries are Sympathetic to Us After Returning From Inspection 274

丨Unemployed Overseas Chinese are Being Repatriated to China in Succession丨

Shen Jinding, Director of the Asian Department of the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, went to Europe last year under the order of the Ministry to participate in the work of the Chinese delegation to the League of Nations in Geneva. After the matter was completed, he also inspected the political situation in various European countries. He arrived in Shanghai yesterday afternoon on the Russian Empress ship and is scheduled to take the night train to Beijing tonight to report. Reporters from the Xinsheng News Agency visited him this morning at his residence. Mr. Shen made the following statement:

Sympathetic to Us Director Shen said that he was ordered to go abroad to attend the League of Nations and assist the Chinese delegation in dealing with the Sino-Japanese issue. He spent four months in Europe. After the League of Nations adjourned, he inspected England, France, Germany, Austria, Holland, Belgium, Italy, Spain, and Portugal, and returned to China in early March to report to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and resume his position as Director of the Asian Department. He has many impressions as a result of inspecting various countries in Europe. However, according to the custom of diplomats, he is not convenient to publish or criticize anything before making a formal report to the government. However, generally speaking, the atmosphere in various countries towards the Chinese issue is the same, sympathetic to us.

Overseas Chinese Returning to China Many overseas Chinese in Europe have recently been affected by the global economic panic. At the same time, due to their limited financial resources or being deceived, many overseas Chinese have been stranded abroad. This situation affects the image of the country. The embassies and consulates abroad are doing their best to repatriate unemployed and stranded overseas Chinese. France, where the number of unemployed overseas Chinese is relatively large, has been repatriated in batches by the embassy in France. The rest, such as Holland and Belgium, are also underway. It is expected that it will be realized soon. The funds are issued by the government.

Anti-Japanese Generals Ma Su Li Wang and Others Leave the Russian Capital and Return to China by Sea 275

丨More Than 10,000 Troops Under His Command Go From Tacheng to Xinjiang to Enter Chahar丨

Today's newspaper reported that Ma Zhanshan, Su Bingwen, and others led more than 10,000 old troops to return to China from Europe, arriving in Tacheng. From Dihua to Ningxia, transportation is quite inconvenient. East of Ningxia, there are highways and the PingSui Railway. In total, the whole journey is quite tortuous. It is not known when they will arrive in Chahar. Ma Su and others decided not to take this route to return to China. They will leave the Russian capital on the 14th of this month and go to Germany, Italy, and other countries to return to China by sea.

The Municipal Government Sends a Letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association to Discuss Factory Inspection Methods 276

Regarding the inspection of factories in this city, the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau has been actively carrying out inspections since the Central Government promulgated the Factory Inspection Law. However, the concession suddenly proposed to carry out its own inspections. The municipal government believes that this matter concerns sovereignty and that factory inspections are part of China's entire labor administration. The concession should not overstep its authority. It has repeatedly sent personnel to negotiate, but without success. The Secretariat of the Municipal Government sent a letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Public Concession yesterday, explaining the importance of factory inspections in the concession being carried out by the Chinese government, and expressed its willingness to sincerely discuss proper methods with the concession authorities within the scope of not conflicting with the Central Government's laws in order to implement the law as soon as possible. The original letter is recorded as follows: The undersigned respectfully states that the Mayor has issued a large letter regarding the proposal of the concession authorities to convene a special meeting of taxpayers to amend Article 34 of the Land Regulations, so as to manage factories. The government has also been instructed to investigate the promulgation of the Factory Law to improve labor conditions and promote harmonious labor-capital relations. Factories in the special zone account for about two-thirds of the city. If they are not implemented at the same time, not only will inspections be impossible to carry out, but factories outside the special zone will also have an excuse. Therefore, personnel have been sent to negotiate repeatedly, but without success. The Municipal Council cannot set separate labor regulations in the special zone for taxpayers to abide by (the Council's legal advisor, Mr. Lai De, said this in 1925). Therefore, it wants to amend the appendices to obtain a legal basis for managing factories. It is not known that inspections are set up to implement China's labor policy, and its purpose is to promote the sound development of the entire national economy, which has nothing to do with local governance. Therefore, the Municipal Council cannot invoke the ninth article of the Yangjingbang Regulations, "Plan ahead for proper management," to seize the power of factory inspections by any means. It must be known that the territorial rights in the concession still belong to our country, and the people in the concession naturally have the same obligation to obey the will of the state as the people living outside the concession. The concession authorities cannot pass a resolution to push the people in the concession outside the power of the state. In short, the government believes that the factory inspection in this city belongs to China's entire labor administration and cannot be abandoned. However, in order to implement this law as soon as possible, it is willing to sincerely discuss proper methods with the concession authorities within the scope of not conflicting with the Central Government's laws, etc. We hereby inform you and ask you to investigate. Sincerely, Shanghai Public Concession Chinese Taxpayers' Association, Shanghai Municipal Government Secretariat.

Searching Pedestrians and Arresting a Gang of Thieves 281

They confessed to being a group of five who planned to rob Yufengxing Grocery Store under Yongxing Tea House on Yongxing Road but failed and were arrested on Yongxing Road. The leader, Yu A'gen (also known as Da Hongzi), was still at large. The Fourth District Police Station has detained Peng Zhengyou and Yang Qicheng and is currently investigating the remaining gang members to bring them to justice.

A Coincidental Encounter with Robbers at Tianyunlou 282

丨The Arrest by Detectives丨

On the morning of the 8th of this month at 10:30 AM, the Tongkang Paint Shop at No. 32 Jinyu Lane, Edward Road, was suddenly invaded by five robbers. Four of them, each holding a pistol, forced the fourteen employees of the shop into one room to guard them and began their robbery. They stole 518.50 yuan in foreign banknotes and 140 yuan in silver dollars from the donation box and counter. Still unsatisfied, they continued to search the employees, seizing five gold watches and 18 yuan in silver dollars, before fleeing. After the shop reported to the Laozha Gate Police Station, yesterday, the police station dispatched Chinese Detective Zhang Yuanqing, detectives Wang Yifei and Weng Hongdong, along with Tongkang's staff Zhang Jialin and Chuan Linfu, to search diligently at various game halls and public places. At 10:30 PM, at the Tianyunlou game hall in the Wing On Company, Zhang and Fu reported to the detectives that they had just seen a tourist wearing a light gray overcoat who was one of the robbers from the shop robbery yesterday. The detectives then went to arrest him and brought him back to the police station. He was identified as Zhang Yingen, also known as Qu Jingen, a Shanghai native. Seventy-five yuan in banknotes, a Hong Kong silver coin, a Heping brand wristwatch, and one yuan in silver dollars were found on him, all of which Fu confirmed as stolen items. The detectives then went to Zhang's residence at No. 65 Fengyu Lane, Route Sapey, in the French Concession and arrested his mistress, Li Ruxun (22 years old, from Songjiang, previously engaged in prostitution). They also seized two gold wristwatches, a gold chain, two gold watches, a long gown, seven pawn tickets, and 134 yuan in banknotes, bringing them back to the police station and detaining them separately. Later, in the French Concession on Route Aigre, they also arrested an accomplice, Xue Lianzhang from Ningbo. This morning, they were jointly transferred to the First Special Court's Criminal Division One. According to the police station's lawyer, Ru Baoyi, who explained the case, Zhang was initially prosecuted under Article 248 of the Criminal Law. The criminal acts of Li and Xue were still under investigation and were permitted to be detained. Judge Qian Hongye briefly questioned the defendants and ordered them to be remanded in custody for further questioning at a later date.

Commentary

Resistance Against Japan and Boycotting Japanese Goods 283

— Geng

The national crisis has reached a point of life and death! "Active military resistance" and "passive economic sanctions" are recognized as the only means to respond to Japanese imperialism. Not only is this known, but it has been repeatedly declared from various angles, with vows to do so. For example, those in power have made "vows" of resistance, "oaths of mobilization," "vows to defend the territory to the death," and "vows not to return alive." Those below have made "vows not to buy," "vows not to sell," and "vows not to use" Japanese goods. Moreover, the significance of "vows" lies not only in showing sincerity and honesty that Heaven and Earth can witness, but also contains a subtle sense of humor, enough to greatly intimidate Japan. It seems that every time a "vow" is made, it is as if pointing to the sky and drawing on the ground, aiming at Japan and saying: "Little Eastern barbarian! I am betting on a curse here, 'cursing' to fight you. Little one, aren't you afraid? Humph! 'Just you try!'"

Unfortunately, the Japanese are really stubborn and bastards. It seems they have clearly learned that these soundless and shapeless, weak "curses" are no different from an old woman's cursing chickens and dogs. Therefore, they consistently maintain an attitude: let you curse, I'll do what I want. After achieving victory, they even announce the facts like "white lice crawling on clothes," "eating people and shaming people," truly unafraid of infuriating those who made the curses!

At the end of last year, newspapers had the following record:

"Recently, the price of Japanese currency has fallen, and the anti-Japanese boycott has invisibly declined. Japanese merchants are vying to import various goods, hoping to make a fortune. In total, Japanese goods imported into this port in one month reached about ten thousand tons."

According to the recent announcement by the Japanese Ministry of Finance, Japan's exports to China (i.e., our imports) in February of this year amounted to 32,263,000 Japanese yen. Although the figures for March have not yet been released, inferring from this huge number, as well as the prosperous business of various stores and the peaceful scene throughout the country, it is better for the Japanese Ministry of Finance to show mercy and not publish the numbers, so as not to scare the patriotic elements who "dare not lag behind others in their love of the country!"

During this intense month of boycotting, so many Japanese goods were re-imported. This must be a new invention of Japanese science, secretly giving Japanese goods wings or four legs, so they automatically "fly" and "run" to stores that have "vowed not to buy" or "sell" Japanese goods, and then "fly" and "run" to the homes of good people who have "vowed not to buy" or "use" Japanese goods! Therefore, the great responsibility of boycotting Japanese goods in the future can only be borne by the Indians, as suggested by a certain diplomat!

As for the anti-Japanese war of "what vows, what vows," how is it going? It only needs to take the obvious facts of the four provinces of Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, and Rehe as the "addend," and then take the recent "denials" with words and the "black squares" without words, the implied meanings commonly seen in the newspapers, as the "addends." A simple "addition" will give us the true "answer" we seek!

Another Shortcut for Converting Silver Taels to Silver Dollars 284

— Wei

After reading Mr. Ouyang's article "A 715 Shortcut for Converting Silver Taels to Silver Dollars" in the April 6 issue of this publication, I find the calculation ingenious and admirable! However, I believe that this type of mnemonic, similar to the flying return in abacus calculations, is difficult to remember without thorough study. Moreover, because it involves too many digits during calculation, it is not easy to apply, and I still feel it has some shortcomings. I now have another shortcut method, briefly described below for the readers' research.

The reason is that when we usually convert silver taels into silver dollars, we need to divide the number of silver taels by the customs duty (洋釐). Because it requires the application of division, the calculation procedure is more troublesome. According to arithmetic principles, dividing number B by number A is exactly equivalent to multiplying number B by the reciprocal of number A (since A / B = B × I / A). Therefore, if you want to convert the number of silver taels into the number of silver dollars, you can multiply the number of silver taels by the reciprocal of the customs duty, so as to avoid the tediousness of the division procedure. For example, if you want to convert 367 taels of treasury silver into silver dollars according to the legally defined customs duty of 715, the formula for using division is as follows:

Number of taels 367

丨丨丨丨丨=513.29 yuan.

Customs duty 0.715

If using multiplication, the formula is as follows: Number of taels ×丨丨=367丨丨=365×1·3 Customs duty 0.715

986=513.29 yuan. The reason is that according to the legally defined customs duty of 715, one tael of treasury silver should be equal to 1.3986 silver dollars. Therefore, when converting silver taels into silver dollars, one should multiply the number of silver taels by 1.3986. The principle is very clear. Now that the customs duty is legally defined, it must not change. Therefore, the number 1.3986 also remains fixed. In order to simplify the calculation procedure, this number can be abbreviated as 1.4. According to this simplified number, the difference from the original real number is only 0.0014 yuan, that is, when using 1.4 to multiply the silver taels to find the number of silver dollars, each tael of silver is calculated to be 1.4 hao of a silver dollar more, a hundred taels calculate one jiao and four fen of a silver dollar more, and a thousand taels calculate one yuan and four jiao more, which can be corrected during conversion. Let's still use the previous question as an example, using the shortcut method to calculate as follows:

367 × 1.4 = 513.80 yuan.

513.80 丨(3.67 × .14) = 513.80 丨.51 = 513.29 yuan.

In the previous formula, 3.67 × .14 is the number of silver dollars over calculated when converting silver taels into silver dollars using 1.4 to multiply the silver taels, so it must be subtracted. The number to be subtracted is the same as the product in the upper half of the previous formula, so there is no need to calculate it. Just move the decimal point up three places. Since the number of silver taels to be converted into silver dollars is in the hundreds, the number to be subtracted should be in the jiao.

In Sickness 285

— Ping

(1) Death

Being sick is not my exclusive privilege. In the experience of every patient, whether it's just a fever or chills, the frightening word "death" easily floats up in their consciousness. My father died of illness, my cousin died of illness, my friend died of illness, how can my illness be an exception? Many terrifying images are gathered around the tent door, and I feel like I might die at any moment, but finally, I get out of bed. All the terrible images of death are driven out of my memory, replaced by bread in my mind. Apart from suicide, death isn't that easy, is it?

(2) Spring

Spring has drifted into the world, and sentimental poets sing beautiful verses, and green willows and peach blossoms are even more praised in words. I seem to remember that it's time to sweep the graves. Drifting at sea for nearly five years, my hometown is thousands of miles away. Is the grass on my father's grave still as lush as when I left? I'm afraid my old mother's head will be covered with frost-like white hair? What does each spring bring me? Adding a mark in age is the path to death. Spring, can you give me one last hope? The sound of a car comes from outside the window, telling me that it is going to Longhua to sweep the graves. I lean on the windowsill, looking southwest, Spring, give me one last hope!
